````
16. # Axion 项目上下文 — AI Agent 实施指南
17. 
18. _本文件包含 AI Agent 在实现 Axion 代码时必须遵循的关键规则和模式。聚焦于容易遗漏的非显而易见的细节。_
19. 
20. ---
21. 
22. ## 技术栈与版本
23. 
24. | 技术 | 版本 | 说明 |
25. |------|------|------|
26. | Swift | 6.1+ | swift-tools-version: 6.1 |
27. | 目标平台 | macOS 14+ (Sonoma) | 需要 AX API 和 SMAppService |
28. | SPM | Swift Package Manager | 唯一包管理器，无 CocoaPods/Carthage |
29. | OpenAgentSDK | 本地依赖 (`../open-agent-sdk-swift`) | path-based SPM 依赖，并行开发 |
30. | swift-mcp | 2.0.0+（fork: terryso/swift-mcp） | Helper 端 MCP Server，AxionHelper 和 AxionCLI 均使用 |
31. | swift-argument-parser | 1.5.0+ | CLI 参数解析 |
32. | Hummingbird | 2.22.0+ | HTTP API Server 框架（Epic 5 新增） |
33. | swift-json-schema | 0.11.0+ | JSONSchemaBuilder，AxionHelper SelectorQuery 使用 |
34. 
35. **关键版本约束：**
36. - `swift-tools-version: 6.1` — 由 OpenAgentSDK 本地依赖决定（SDK 要求 6.1+）
37. - `macOS 14+` 是硬性要求，不能降低（AX API 变更、SMAppService）
38. - OpenAgentSDK 是本地 path 依赖，不是远程 URL — 修改 SDK 后 Axion 无需更新依赖声明
39. - 无 Node.js/Python 依赖 — 纯 Swift 静态编译
40. 
41. **NFR 性能指标（实现时必须满足）：**
42. 
43. | 指标 | 目标 | 来源 |
44. |------|------|------|
45. | CLI 冷启动到首次 LLM 请求发出 | < 2 秒 | NFR1 |
46. | AxionHelper 启动到 MCP 连接就绪 | < 500ms | NFR2 |
47. | 单个 AX 操作（MCP 请求到结果返回） | < 200ms | NFR3 |
48. | CLI 进程常驻内存 | < 30MB | NFR4 |
49. | Helper 进程常驻内存 | < 20MB | NFR4 |
50. | AxionBar 常驻内存 | < 15MB | NFR32 |
51. | 全局热键响应延迟 | < 200ms | NFR35 |
52. | 技能执行首步延迟 | < 100ms | NFR31 |
53. | AxionCLI 源码总行数 | ≤ 10,688（重构后） | NFR51 |
54. | AxionCLI 桌面专属代码占比 | ≥ 70% | NFR52 |
55. | API/ 使用 SDK 底层组件 | RunTracker、EventBroadcaster 保留 Axion 专属端点 | NFR53 |
56. | ToolRegistrar.swift | ≤ 200 行，工具注册分布在 7 个分类文件 | NFR54 |
57. | Memory 通用逻辑来自 SDK | Axion 保留 8 个桌面专属文件 | NFR55 |
58. | CostTracker/TraceRecorder | SDK Agent 内建管理（AgentOptions），Axion 不自建 actor | NFR56 |
59. 
60. ---
61. 
62. ## 语言规则（Swift）
63. 
64. ### 命名规范（三套规则，互不冲突）
65. 
66. **Swift 代码命名：**
67. - 类型（struct/enum/class/protocol）：PascalCase → `AxionConfig`, `Skill`, `MCPClientProtocol`
68. - 函数和方法：camelCase，动词开头 → `buildAgent()`, `loadPrompt()`
69. - 属性和变量：camelCase → `maxSteps`, `currentPlan`
70. - 枚举 case：camelCase → `.done`, `.needsClarification`
71. - 协议：名词 + `Protocol` 后缀 → `MCPClientProtocol`, `Configurable`
72. - 文件名：与主类型同名 → `Skill.swift`, `Value.swift`
73. - 目录名：PascalCase 复数 → `Commands/`, `Services/`, `Models/`
74. 
75. **MCP 工具命名（跨进程通信）：**
76. - snake_case → `launch_app`, `type_text`, `press_key`
77. - 动词 + 名词 → `click`, `scroll`, `get_window_state`
78. - 工具名必须与 `ToolNames.swift` 常量保持一致
79. 
80. **JSON 字段命名：**
81. - MCP 请求/响应参数：snake_case → `{"app_name": "Calculator"}`
82. - Config 文件（Codable 默认）：camelCase → `{"maxSteps": 20}`
83. - Trace 事件：snake_case → `{"event": "step_done"}`
84. 
85. ### Import 顺序（严格遵守）
86. 
87. ```swift
88. // 1. 系统框架
89. import Foundation
90. import Security
91. 
92. // 2. 第三方依赖
93. import ArgumentParser
94. import OpenAgentSDK
95. import Hummingbird    // Epic 5+ HTTP API Server
96. import NIOCore        // ByteBuffer (SSE/Hummingbird)
97. import MCP
98. import MCPTool
99. 
100. // 3. 项目内部模块
101. import AxionCore
102. ```
103. 
104. ### 模型定义规范
105. 
106. - 所有共享模型放在 `AxionCore/` — 遵循 `Codable + Equatable` 一致性
107. - 枚举使用 `String` 原始值以支持 Codable → `enum ConnectionStatus: String, Codable`
108. - 复杂枚举编码使用 `{type, value}` 模式（参见 `Value.swift`）
109. - Config 使用 camelCase JSON 键 — `CodingKeys` 不做转换，依赖 Swift 默认行为
110. - **部分 JSON 解码规范**：Codable 模型的 `init(from decoder:)` 使用 `decodeIfPresent` + `?? Self.default.xxx`，使缺失字段自动回退到默认值。新增字段时只需在此 init 中加一行，调用方无需修改。
111. 
112. ### 错误处理
113. 
114. - 统一使用 `AxionError` 枚举，**不创建新的错误类型体系**
115. - 每个错误 case 必须提供 `MCPErrorPayload`（含 `error`/`message`/`suggestion` 三字段）
116. - MCP ToolResult 中的错误 JSON 必须是 `{"error": "...", "message": "...", "suggestion": "..."}`
117. - 使用 `toToolResultJSON()` 生成格式化的错误输出，`JSONEncoder.outputFormatting = [.sortedKeys, .prettyPrinted]`
118. 
119. ### 日志级别
120.
````

</details>

<summary>94 lines</summary>

````
241. ## 测试规则
242. 
243. ### 测试命名格式
244. 
245. ```swift
246. // 格式：test_被测单元_场景_预期结果
247. func test_plan_codable_roundTrip_preservesAllFields() throws
248. func test_value_placeholder_preservesDollarSign() throws
249. func test_error_toToolResultJSON_containsRequiredFields() throws
250. ```
251. 
252. ### 测试组织
253. 
254. - 测试文件镜像源文件结构
255. - 使用 `// MARK: - 分组描述` 组织测试方法
256. - 测试类命名：`{被测类型}Tests` → `PlanTests`, `AxionErrorTests`
257. 
258. ### 测试模式
259. 
260. **Codable round-trip 测试**（核心模式 — 几乎所有模型都有）：
261. ```swift
262. func test_xxx_roundTrip() throws {
263.     let original = ...
264.     let data = try JSONEncoder().encode(original)
265.     let decoded = try JSONDecoder().decode(X.self, from: data)
266.     XCTAssertEqual(decoded, original)
267. }
268. ```
269. 
270. **ATDD 分级标注**（在测试类注释中标注优先级）：
271. ```swift
272. // [P0] 基础设施验证
273. // [P1] 行为验证
274. ```
275. 
276. **Mock 策略：**
277. - 通过 Protocol 注入 Mock（`MCPClientProtocol`, `AgentBuilderProtocol` 等）
278. - 不 Mock 的层：AxionCore 模型（纯数据）、JSON 编解码（直接 round-trip）
279. - 单元测试禁止真实系统调用（NSWorkspace、CGEvent、网络请求等），必须通过 mock/protocol 隔离
280. - 涉及真实系统调用的测试（`*RealTests`）必须放在 `Tests/**/Integration/` 目录，由 `make test-integration` 运行，不混入 `make test`
281. 
282. **Helper 测试层级：**
283. - 进程级冒烟测试（`HelperProcessSmokeTests`）— 启动真实进程测试 MCP JSON-RPC
284. - 内存级集成测试（`HelperMCPServerTests`）— 不启动进程，直接测试 MCPServer API
285. - 脚手架测试（`HelperScaffoldTests`）— 验证模块导入和类型存在性
286. 
287. ---
288. 
289. ## 并发模式
290. 
291. ### Actor 隔离边界
292. 
293. | Actor | 职责 | 隔离原因 |
294. |-------|------|----------|
295. | `HelperProcessManager` | Helper 进程启停、MCP 连接 | 进程状态串行化 |
296. | `MCPConnection` | JSON-RPC 收发 | stdio 管道不能并发读写 |
297. | `TraceRecorder` | Trace 事件写入（thin SDK integration layer, 308 lines） | 文件写入串行化（SDK AgentOptions 内建管理 trace/cost） |
298. | `AxionRunTracker` | HTTP API 任务状态管理（wraps SDK RunTracker） | 任务状态串行化，每次状态变更持久化 |
299. | `EventBroadcaster` | SSE 事件多客户端广播 + 事件持久化 | 订阅者和重放缓存串行化，每次 emit 追加到 api-events.jsonl |
300. | `ConcurrencyLimiter` | 并发任务槽位管理（SDK 提供） | 并发计数和排队串行化 |
301. | `TaskQueue` | MCP Server 模式任务串行化（SDK 提供） | agent.prompt() 调用串行化 |
302. | `GatewayRunner` | Gateway 生命周期管理、任务调度 | 进程状态、启停、信号处理串行化（D9） |
303. | `TelegramAdapter` | TG Bot API 长轮询、消息收发 | TG API 调用和消息队列串行化（D10） |
304. | `ReviewScheduler` | 后台审查调度 | 审查间隔状态串行化（D11） |
305. | `CuratorScheduler` | Curator 自动调度 | 空闲计时和 curator 状态串行化（D11） |
306. 
307. ### Helper 进程生命周期（D8）
308. 
309. 1. CLI 首次需要 AX 操作时，`HelperProcessManager.start()` 启动 Helper
310. 2. 通过 `Process.standardInput` / `standardOutput` 建立 stdio 管道
311. 3. `DispatchGroup` 跟踪 Helper 进程存活状态
312. 4. **优雅终止流程**：发送 SIGTERM → 等待最多 3 秒 → 超时则 SIGKILL
313. 5. 注册 SIGINT handler，Ctrl-C 时传播到 Helper（NFR8）
314. 6. Helper 意外崩溃时，检测到后尝试**重启一次**
315. 
316. ### Task 取消传播
317. 
318. ```swift
319. try await withTaskCancellationHandler {
320.     try await executor.execute(plan: plan)
321. } onCancel: {
322.     Task { await helperManager.stop() }
323. }
324. ```
325. 
326. ### 重试策略
327. 
328. - 仅用于 LLM API 调用和 transient MCP 错误
329. - 指数退避：1s → 2s → 4s
330. - **不**用于业务逻辑错误（如"应用未找到"）
331. 
332. ---
333. 
334. ## 关键反模式（必须避免）
````

</details>

/Users/nick/CascadeProjects/codex/README.md (lines 1-260)

````
1. <p align="center"><strong>Codex CLI</strong> is a coding agent from OpenAI that runs locally on your computer.
2. <p align="center">
3.   <img src="https://github.com/openai/codex/blob/main/.github/codex-cli-splash.png" alt="Codex CLI splash" width="80%" />
4. </p>
5. </br>
6. If you want Codex in your code editor (VS Code, Cursor, Windsurf), <a href="https://developers.openai.com/codex/ide">install in your IDE.</a>
7. </br>If you want the desktop app experience, run <code>codex app</code> or visit <a href="https://chatgpt.com/codex?app-landing-page=true">the Codex App page</a>.
8. </br>If you are looking for the <em>cloud-based agent</em> from OpenAI, <strong>Codex Web</strong>, go to <a href="https://chatgpt.com/codex">chatgpt.com/codex</a>.</p>
9. 
10. ---
11. 
12. ## Quickstart
13. 
14. ### Installing and running Codex CLI
15. 
16. Run the following on Mac or Linux to install Codex CLI:
17. 
18. ```shell
19. curl -fsSL https://chatgpt.com/codex/install.sh | sh
20. ```
21. 
22. Run the following on Windows to install Codex CLI:
23. 
24. ```
25. powershell -ExecutionPolicy ByPass -c "irm https://chatgpt.com/codex/install.ps1 | iex"
26. ```
27. 
28. Codex CLI can also be installed via the following package managers:
29. 
30. ```shell
31. # Install using npm
32. npm install -g @openai/codex
33. ```
34. 
35. ```shell
36. # Install using Homebrew
37. brew install --cask codex
38. ```
39. 
40. Then simply run `codex` to get started.
41. 
42. <details>
43. <summary>You can also go to the <a href="https://github.com/openai/codex/releases/latest">latest GitHub Release</a> and download the appropriate binary for your platform.</summary>
44. 
45. Each GitHub Release contains many executables, but in practice, you likely want one of these:
46. 
47. - macOS
48.   - Apple Silicon/arm64: `codex-aarch64-apple-darwin.tar.gz`
49.   - x86_64 (older Mac hardware): `codex-x86_64-apple-darwin.tar.gz`
50. - Linux
51.   - x86_64: `codex-x86_64-unknown-linux-musl.tar.gz`
52.   - arm64: `codex-aarch64-unknown-linux-musl.tar.gz`
53. 
54. Each archive contains a single entry with the platform baked into the name (e.g., `codex-x86_64-unknown-linux-musl`), so you likely want to rename it to `codex` after extracting it.
55. 
56. </details>
57. 
58. ### Using Codex with your ChatGPT plan
59. 
60. Run `codex` and select **Sign in with ChatGPT**. We recommend signing into your ChatGPT account to use Codex as part of your Plus, Pro, Business, Edu, or Enterprise plan. [Learn more about what's included in your ChatGPT plan](https://help.openai.com/en/articles/11369540-codex-in-chatgpt).
61. 
62. You can also use Codex with an API key, but this requires [additional setup](https://developers.openai.com/codex/auth#sign-in-with-an-api-key).
63. 
64. ## Docs
65. 
66. - [**Codex Documentation**](https://developers.openai.com/codex)
67. - [**Contributing**](./docs/contributing.md)
68. - [**Installing & building**](./docs/install.md)
69. - [**Open source fund**](./docs/open-source-fund.md)
70. 
71. This repository is licensed under the [Apache-2.0 License](LICENSE).
72.

<sub>⏱️ 4m 56s</sub>

### ✅ `view`

**view the file at /Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/docs/epics/epic-37-interactive-chat-mode.md.**

/Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/docs/epics/epic-37-interactive-chat-mode.md (lines 1-260)

<details>
<summary>260 lines</summary>

````
1. # Axion Epic 37: 交互聊天模式
2. 
3. > **状态：待开发**
4. > **优先级：P0**
5. > **前置依赖：无（ChatCommand 已在 feat/interactive-chat 分支实现 MVP）**
6. > **技术验证：** 快速验证已完成，MVP 分支 `feat/interactive-chat`
7. 
8. ## 背景与动机
9. 
10. Axion 的 `run` 命令是单次执行模式（`axion run "task"`），类似 `claude -p`。Epic 37 的目标是让 `axion` 无参数直接进入交互式多轮 REPL，成为类似 Claude Code 的 coding agent。
11. 
12. **MVP 已完成（feat/interactive-chat 分支）：**
13. - `ChatCommand.swift` — 交互 REPL，`axion` 无参数进入
14. - `agent.stream()` 每轮调用，流式输出
15. - `SessionStore` 会话持久化
16. - MCP 连接复用（SDK 0.7.6 修复）
17. - 工具验证通过：Read、Edit、Write、Bash、Glob、Grep
18. 
19. **MVP 的限制（本 Epic 要解决的）：**
20. - System Prompt 是桌面自动化的 `planner-system`（含 screenshot、list_apps），不适合 coding agent
21. - 无 CLAUDE.md / 项目级指令加载
22. - 输出是纯文本 `[axion]` 前缀格式，无 Markdown 渲染
23. - 只有 `/exit` 命令，缺少 `/help`、`/clear`、`/compact` 等
24. - 无权限审批，所有操作直接执行（当前 `permissionMode: .bypassPermissions`）
25. - `readLine()` 不支持多行输入和粘贴
26. - Ctrl+C 会杀死进程而非中断当前任务
27. - 中文输入 backspace 删除字符需要按两次
28. - `maxTokens=4096` 太小，coding agent 回复经常超限
29. - 无上下文用量提示，长对话可能 token 溢出
30. - 无会话恢复能力，退出后对话丢失
31. - 启动信息不足（缺模型、工作目录、session ID）
32. 
33. ---
34. 
35. ## 全局参数约定
36. 
37. 本 Epic 所有 Story 共享以下默认参数，在 `ChatCommand` 的 `BuildConfig` 中生效：
38. 
39. | 参数 | 值 | 说明 |
40. |------|-----|------|
41. | 上下文窗口 | 200K tokens | 通过 `maxModelContextTokens` 配置 |
42. | 最大输出 token | 128K | 通过 `maxTokens` 配置（MVP 是 4096） |
43. | 自动压缩阈值 | 80%（160K） | 上下文达到 80% 时自动 compact |
44. | PermissionMode | `.default` | 危险操作需确认（MVP 是 `.bypassPermissions`） |
45. | System Prompt | coding-agent-system | 独立 prompt 模板，非桌面自动化的 planner-system |
46. 
47. ---
48. 
49. ### Story 37.0: Coding Agent 系统提示 + 项目上下文
50. 
51. As a coding agent 用户,
52. I want 交互模式使用专为代码编写优化的系统提示，并自动加载项目级指令,
53. So that agent 理解 coding 场景并遵循项目约定.
54. 
55. **当前问题：** `forCLI()` 使用 `buildSystemPrompt()` 加载 `planner-system` 模板（面向桌面自动化，含 screenshot、list_apps、accessibility tree 等指令）。交互模式需要自己的系统提示。
56. 
57. **实施：**
58. 
59. 1. 新建 `Resources/prompts/coding-agent-system.md` 系统提示模板，核心内容：
60. 
61. ```
62. 你是 Axion，一个运行在终端的 AI coding agent。
63. 
64. ## 核心能力
65. - 读写文件（Read、Write、Edit）
66. - 执行命令（Bash）
67. - 搜索代码（Grep、Glob）
68. - 代码智能（LSP：定义跳转、引用查找、类型信息）
69. - 网络搜索（WebSearch、WebFetch）
70. 
71. ## 工作原则
72. 1. 先理解再动手 — 用 Read/Grep/Glob 了解上下文后再修改代码
73. 2. 小步修改 — 每次只做必要的改动，避免大范围重构
74. 3. 验证结果 — 修改后运行相关测试确认
75. 4. 保持安全 — 不引入注入、XSS 等安全漏洞
76. 5. 遵循项目约定 — 写代码前先了解项目的命名、架构、测试习惯
77. 
78. ## 输出格式
79. - 每轮回复末尾包含一行总结：`[结果] <一句话摘要，最多100字>`
80. - 工具调用时简要说明目的
81. - 代码修改说明改了什么和为什么
82. ```
83. 
84. 2. 新建 `buildCodingSystemPrompt()` 方法（或在 `buildSystemPrompt` 中加 `mode` 参数）
85. 
86. ```swift
87. // AgentBuilder.swift 新增
88. private static func buildCodingSystemPrompt(
89.     config: AxionConfig,
90.     cwd: String,
91.     memoryStore: FileBasedMemoryStore,
92.     memoryDir: String,
93.     skillRegistry: SkillRegistry,
94.     noMemory: Bool,
95.     noSkills: Bool
96. ) async -> String {
97.     let promptDir = PromptBuilder.resolvePromptDirectory()
98.     let basePrompt = (try? PromptBuilder.load(
99.         name: "coding-agent-system",
100.         variables: ["cwd": cwd],
101.         fromDirectory: promptDir
102.     )) ?? ""
103. 
104.     // Memory context（复用现有逻辑）
105.     var memoryContext: String? = nil
106.     if !noMemory { ... }
107. 
108.     // CLAUDE.md 加载
109.     let claudeMdContext = loadClaudeMd(cwd: cwd)
110. 
111.     let skillsPrompt = noSkills ? "" : skillRegistry.formatSkillsForPrompt()
112.     return buildFullSystemPrompt(...)
113. }
114. ```
115. 
116. 3. **CLAUDE.md 加载** — 扫描以下路径，按优先级合并：
117.    - `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` — 全局指令
118.    - `<project-root>/.claude/CLAUDE.md` — 项目级团队指令
119.    - `<project-root>/CLAUDE.md` — 项目根目录指令
120.    - `<project-root>/.axion/instructions.md` — Axion 专用指令
121. 
122. ```swift
123. static func loadClaudeMd(cwd: String) -> String {
124.     var parts: [String] = []
125.     let candidates = [
126.         NSHomeDirectory() + "/.claude/CLAUDE.md",
127.         cwd + "/.claude/CLAUDE.md",
128.         cwd + "/CLAUDE.md",
129.         cwd + "/.axion/instructions.md"
130.     ]
131.     for path in candidates {
132.         if let content = try? String(contentsOfFile: path),
133.            !content.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces).isEmpty {
134.             parts.append("## 指令 (\(URL(fileURLWithPath: path).lastPathComponent))\n\(content)")
135.         }
136.     }
137.     return parts.joined(separator: "\n\n")
138. }
139. ```
140. 
141. 4. 在 `BuildConfig.forCLI()` 中根据 `mode` 参数选择不同的 prompt 构建路径
142. 5. `maxTokens` 从 4096 改为 128K
143. 6. `permissionMode` 从 `.bypassPermissions` 改为 `.default`
144. 
145. **新增文件：**
146. - `Resources/prompts/coding-agent-system.md`
147. 
148. **修改文件：**
149. - `Sources/AxionCLI/Services/AgentBuilder.swift` — 新增 `buildCodingSystemPrompt()`，`BuildConfig` 加 `mode` 字段
150. 
151. **Acceptance Criteria：**
152. 
153. **Given** 用户在 axion 项目目录下运行 `axion`
154. **When** agent 启动
155. **Then** system prompt 使用 `coding-agent-system` 模板（不包含 screenshot、list_apps 等桌面自动化指令）
156. **And** `CLAUDE.md` 内容被注入 system prompt
157. 
158. **Given** 项目根目录存在 `CLAUDE.md` 内容为 "所有测试用 Swift Testing 框架"
159. **When** agent 执行编码任务
160. **Then** agent 遵循该约定，生成 `@Test` 而非 `XCTestCase` 测试
161. 
162. **Given** `maxTokens` 设为 128K
163. **When** agent 生成较长的代码回复
164. **Then** 回复不会被截断（对比 MVP 中 maxTokens=4096 时的截断问题）
165. 
166. ---
167. 
168. ### Story 37.1: Slash 命令体系
169. 
170. As a CLI 用户,
171. I want 在交互模式中使用 /help、/clear、/compact 等斜杠命令,
172. So that 我可以控制对话行为而不用退出重进.
173. 
174. **Slash 命令清单：**
175. 
176. | 命令 | 功能 | 说明 |
177. |------|------|------|
178. | `/help` | 显示帮助 | 列出所有可用命令和快捷键 |
179. | `/clear` | 清屏 | 清除终端输出，不重置会话 |
180. | `/compact` | 压缩上下文 | 手动触发上下文压缩（SDK 已有 compact 机制） |
181. | `/model` | 显示/切换模型 | 无参数显示当前模型，带参数切换 |
182. | `/cost` | 显示用量 | 显示当前会话 token 用量和成本 |
183. | `/resume` | 恢复会话 | 无参数列出最近会话供选择，输入序号恢复（见 Story 37.8） |
184. | `/exit` `/quit` | 退出 | 已实现 |
185. | `/config` | 显示配置 | 显示当前生效的关键配置项 |
186. 
187. **实施：**
188. 
189. 1. 新建 `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/SlashCommand.swift`
190. 
191. ```swift
192. enum SlashCommand {
193.     case help
194.     case clear
195.     case compact
196.     case model(String?)
197.     case cost
198.     case resume  // 无参数：列出会话供选择
199.     case config
200.     case exit
201. 
202.     static func parse(_ input: String) -> SlashCommand? {
203.         let parts = input.split(separator: " ", maxSplits: 1)
204.         let cmd = String(parts[0]).lowercased()
205.         let arg = parts.count > 1 ? String(parts[1]) : nil
206.         switch cmd {
207.         case "/help": return .help
208.         case "/clear": return .clear
209.         case "/compact": return .compact
210.         case "/model": return .model(arg)
211.         case "/cost": return .cost
212.         case "/sessions": return .sessions
213.         case "/resume": return .resume
214.         case "/config": return .config
215.         case "/exit", "/quit": return .exit
216.         default: return nil
217.         }
218.     }
219. }
220. ```
221. 
222. 2. 修改 `ChatCommand.swift` 的 REPL 循环，在 `agent.stream()` 之前检查 slash 命令
223. 
224. ```swift
225. if let cmd = SlashCommand.parse(trimmed) {
226.     handleSlashCommand(cmd, buildResult: &buildResult)
227.     if case .exit = cmd { break }
228.     continue
229. }
230. ```
231. 
232. 3. `handleSlashCommand` 方法处理各命令
233. 
234. **Token 用量数据来源：**
235. - SDK 的 `SDKMessage.result` 包含 `numTurns`、`durationMs`
236. - LLM API response 中有 `usage.prompt_tokens` / `usage.completion_tokens`
237. - 需要在 ChatCommand 中维护一个 `TokenCounter`，从每次 stream 结束后的 result 事件中累计
238. - 如果 SDK 不暴露 token 计数，从 `SessionStore` 的 transcript 大小估算
239. 
240. **Acceptance Criteria：**
241. 
242. **Given** 用户在交互模式中输入 `/help`
243. **When** 命令执行
244. **Then** 显示所有可用 slash 命令列表
245. 
246. **Given** 用户输入 `/clear`
247. **When** 命令执行
248. **Then** 终端清屏，会话历史不变，下一轮对话仍记得上下文
249. 
250. **Given** 用户输入 `/model`
251. **When** 命令执行
252. **Then** 显示当前使用的模型名称
253. 
254. **Given** 用户输入 `/model gpt-4o`
255. **When** 命令执行
256. **Then** 切换模型并确认
257. 
258. **Given** 用户输入 `/cost`
259. **When** 命令执行
260. **Then** 显示当前会话累计 token 数和预估成本
````

</details>

263. 
264. ### Story 37.2: Ctrl+C 优雅中断
265. 
266. As a CLI 用户,
267. I want 按 Ctrl+C 时只中断当前正在执行的任务而不是退出整个交互模式,
268. So that 我可以取消一个耗时操作但继续在同一会话中工作.
269. 
270. **实施：**
271. 
272. 1. 注册 SIGINT 信号处理器，在 REPL 循环外捕获
273. 
274. ```swift
275. import Darwin
276. 
277. var interrupted = false
278. let sigintSrc = DispatchSource.makeSignalSource(signal: SIGINT, queue: .main)
279. signal(SIGINT, SIG_IGN)
280. sigintSrc.setEventHandler { interrupted = true }
281. sigintSrc.resume()
282. ```
283. 
284. 2. 在 `ChatCommand` 中维护 `currentStreamTask: Task<Void, Never>?`
285. 3. Ctrl+C 时 cancel 当前 Task，但保持 REPL 循环
286. 4. 连续两次 Ctrl+C（2 秒内）退出程序
287. 
288. ```swift
289. // REPL loop
290. while true {
291.     fputs("axion> ", stdout); fflush(stdout)
292.     guard let line = readLine(strippingNewline: true) else { break }
293.     // ...
294.     interrupted = false
295.     let streamTask = Task {
296.         for await message in buildResult.agent.stream(trimmed) {
297.             guard !Task.isCancelled else { return }
298.             outputHandler.handle(message)
299.         }
300.     }
301.     // 等待完成或中断
302.     await streamTask.value
303. }
304. ```
305. 
306. **Acceptance Criteria：**
307. 
308. **Given** agent 正在执行一个耗时任务
309. **When** 用户按一次 Ctrl+C
310. **Then** 当前任务被中断，显示 `[axion] 已中断`，回到 `axion>` 提示符
311. **And** 会话历史保留，可以继续对话
312. 
313. **Given** 用户在 2 秒内连续按两次 Ctrl+C
314. **When** 第二次 Ctrl+C
315. **Then** 退出交互模式，显示 `[axion] 再见`
316. 
317. **Given** 用户在 `axion>` 提示符下按 Ctrl+C

366. ### Story 37.4: 终端输出优化
367. 
368. As a CLI 用户,
369. I want 看到更清晰的输出格式——工具结果有摘要、LLM 回复有 Markdown 渲染、进度有动态指示,
370. So that 交互体验更接近 Claude Code 的水平.
371. 
372. **改进项：**
373. 
374. 1. **工具调用格式优化** — 当前 `[axion] 执行: Bash` / `[axion] 结果: ...`
375.    改为缩进层级显示：
376.    ```
377.    ⏳ Bash: echo hello
378.    ✅ hello [120ms]
379.    ```
380. 
381. 2. **LLM 回复直接输出** — 当前通过 `[axion]` 前缀包裹，改为直接在终端输出 LLM 文本，用空行分隔工具调用和回复
382. 
383. 3. **进度指示** — LLM 等待时显示 spinner（`⠋⠙⠹⠸⠼⠴⠦⠧⠇⠏`），工具执行时显示工具名 + spinner
384. 
385. 4. **Markdown 简易渲染** — 对 LLM 回复中的 code block、bold、link 做基本终端渲染（ANSI 转义码）
386.    - `**bold**` → `\033[1mbold\033[0m`
387.    - `` `code` `` → `\033[36mcode\033[0m`
388.    - ```` ```code block``` ```` → 缩进 + 语法提示
389.

393. 2. 新建 `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/MarkdownTerminalRenderer.swift`
394. 3. 修改 `ChatCommand.swift` 使用新的格式化器替代 `SDKTerminalOutputHandler`
395. 
396. **注意：** 不修改 `SDKTerminalOutputHandler`，它被 `RunCommand` 使用。Chat 模式有独立的输出格式化。
397. 
398. **Acceptance Criteria：**
399. 
400. **Given** agent 执行了一个 Bash 命令
401. **When** 结果返回
402. **Then** 显示工具名 + 状态图标 + 结果摘要 + 耗时
403. 
404. **Given** LLM 返回包含 `**bold**` 和 `` `code` `` 的文本
405. **When** 渲染到终端
406. **Then** bold 用粗体显示，code 用不同颜色显示
407. 
408. **Given** LLM 正在思考

410. **Then** 显示动态 spinner
411. 
412. ---
413. 
414. ### Story 37.5: 权限审批机制
415. 
416. As a CLI 用户,
417. I want 在执行危险操作（文件覆盖、删除命令等）前收到确认提示,
418. So that 我可以防止意外破坏.
419. 
420. **实施：**
421. 
422. 1. 将 `ChatCommand` 的 `permissionMode` 从 `.bypassPermissions` 改为 `.default`
423. 2. 使用 SDK 已有的 `PermissionMode` 机制（`.default` 模式会触发 `permissionRequest` hook）
424. 3. 在 `ChatCommand` 中注册 `permissionRequest` 事件处理
425. 
426. ```swift
427. case .hookResponse(let data):
428.     if data.event == "permissionRequest" {
429.         // 显示操作详情，等待用户确认
430.         fputs("⚠️  即将执行: \(data.toolName) — \(data.description)\n", stderr)
431.         fputs("   允许？[y/n] ", stderr)
432.         fflush(stderr)
433.         if let answer = readLine(strippingNewline: true),
434.            answer.lowercased() == "y" {
435.             // approve
436.         }
437.     }
438. ```
439. 
440. 4. 支持三种模式（通过命令行 flag 选择）：
441.    - `--accept-edits` — 自动允许文件编辑，危险 Bash 仍需确认（对应 SDK `.acceptEdits`）
442.    - `--dangerously-skip-permissions` — 全部自动通过（当前 MVP 行为，对应 SDK `.bypassPermissions`）
443.    - 默认（不加 flag）— 写文件、危险 Bash 命令需确认（对应 SDK `.default`）
444. 
445. **危险操作判断规则（SDK 层面）：**
446. - Write/Edit：目标文件已存在 → 需确认
447. - Bash：命令含 `rm`、`drop`、`delete`、`truncate`、`force` → 需确认
448. - Read/Grep/Glob：无需确认
449. 
450. **Acceptance Criteria：**
451. 
452. **Given** 默认模式下 agent 要执行 `rm -rf /tmp/test`
453. **When** 权限请求触发
454. **Then** 终端显示确认提示，用户输入 `y` 后执行，`n` 后跳过
455. 
456. **Given** `--accept-edits` 模式下 agent 要写入已存在的文件
457. **When** 权限请求触发
458. **Then** 自动通过，无需确认
459. 
460. **Given** 默认模式下 agent 要执行 Read 工具
461. **When** 权限请求触发
462. **Then** 自动通过，无需确认
463. 
464. ---
465. 
466. ### Story 37.6: 多行输入支持
467. 
468. As a CLI 用户,
469. I want 能粘贴多行代码片段或用反斜杠续行,
470. So that 我可以输入复杂的 prompt 而不需要写成一行.
471. 
472. **实施：**
473. 
474. 1. 检测 stdin 是否为 TTY（`isatty(STDIN_FILENO)`）
475. 2. 在 TTY 模式下检测粘贴事件（bracket paste mode）
476. 
477. ```swift
478. // 启用 bracket paste mode
479.  fputs("\u{1B}[?2004h", stderr)  // 开启
480.  // 退出时恢复
481.  fputs("\u{1B}[?2004l", stderr)  // 关闭
482. ```
483. 
484. 3. bracket paste 内容用 `\u{1B}[200~` 和 `\u{1B}[201~` 包裹，识别后合并为单条输入
485. 4. 手动续行：行末 `\` + 回车 → 继续读取下一行，合并后发送
486. 
487. **Acceptance Criteria：**
488. 
489. **Given** 用户在 `axion>` 提示符下输入 `print(\` 然后按回车
490. **When** 下一行显示 `...>` 续行提示
491. **Then** 用户继续输入 `)` 后回车，两行合并发送给 agent
492. 
493. **Given** 用户从剪贴板粘贴一段多行代码
494. **When** 粘贴完成
495. **Then** 整段代码作为一条消息发送给 agent，而非按行拆分
496. 
497. ---
498. 
499. ### Story 37.7: 上下文管理
500. 
501. As a CLI 用户,
502. I want 知道当前上下文使用量，且长对话能自动压缩,
503. So that 对话不会因 token 溢出而失败.
504. 
505. **全局参数（Story 37.0 设定）：**
506. - 上下文窗口：200K tokens
507. - 自动压缩阈值：80%（160K tokens）
508. 
509. **实施：**
510. 
511. 1. 上下文用量估算：
512.    - 每轮 stream 结束后，从 `SessionStore` 加载 transcript
513.    - 累计计算消息的字符数，按 1 token ≈ 4 chars 估算
514.    - 或从 LLM API response 的 `usage` 字段提取精确值（如果 SDK 暴露）
515. 
516. 2. 自动 compact：
517.    - 在每轮 stream 开始前检查上下文用量
518.    - 如果 ≥160K tokens，自动触发 compact
519.    - Compact 策略：保留最近 3 轮完整对话 + system prompt，更早的对话压缩为摘要
520.    - 使用 SDK 已有的 compact 机制
`````

543. ### Story 37.8: 会话恢复
544. 
545. As a CLI 用户,
546. I want 能恢复之前的交互会话继续对话,
547. So that 我关掉终端后不用从头开始.
548. 
549. **当前状态：**
550. - 已有 `ResumeCommand`（`axion resume <sessionId>`），但它走 `AxionRuntime` 路径，不支持交互模式
551. - ChatCommand 每次创建新 session（`chat-{UUID}`），退出后 session 保存在 `~/.axion/sessions/`
552. 
553. **实施：**
554. 
555. 1. **`/resume` 命令** — 无参数列出最近会话，用户输入序号选择恢复
556. 
557. ```
558. axion> /resume
559. 最近会话:
560.   1. chat-a3f8b2c1  2026-06-07 13:15  5轮
561.   2. chat-7e4f9d0a  2026-06-07 10:30  12轮
562.   3. chat-1b2c3d4e  2026-06-06 22:00  3轮
563. 
564. 选择要恢复的会话 (1-3, 或 Enter 取消): 2
565. [axion] 已恢复会话 chat-7e4f9d0a（12轮历史）
566. axion>
567. ```
568. 
569. 2. **会话列表扫描** — 读取 `~/.axion/sessions/` 目录，按修改时间倒序，取最近 10 个，从 transcript.json 中读取轮数
570. 
571. ```swift
572. func listRecentSessions(limit: Int = 10) -> [(id: String, date: Date, turns: Int)] {
573.     let sessionsDir = NSHomeDirectory() + "/.axion/sessions"
574.     // scan directory, sort by modificationDate, read transcript for turn count
575. }
576. ```
577. 
578. 3. **恢复流程** — 用户选择后：
579.    - 当前 agent 关闭
580.    - 用选中的 sessionId 重新 build agent（SessionStore 自动加载历史）
581.    - 后续对话在恢复的会话上下文中继续
582. 
583. 4. **命令行快速恢复** — `axion --resume <sessionId>` 跳过选择，直接恢复指定会话
584. 
585. ```swift
586. // ChatCommand 新增参数
587. @Option(name: .long, help: "恢复指定会话 ID")

589. ```

597. **Acceptance Criteria：**
598. 
599. **Given** 用户在交互模式中输入 `/resume`
600. **When** 命令执行
601. **Then** 显示最近 10 个会话（序号、ID 缩写、时间、轮数）
602. **And** 用户输入序号后恢复对应会话
603. **And** 后续对话能引用恢复会话的上下文
604. 
605. **Given** 用户运行 `axion --resume chat-a3f8b2c1`
606. **When** 进入交互模式
607. **Then** 历史对话已加载，第一轮回复能引用之前的上下文
608. 
609. **Given** `/resume` 显示会话列表后
610. **When** 用户按 Enter（不输入序号）
611. **Then** 取消恢复，回到 `axion>` 提示符，当前会话不变
612. 
613. **Given** 用户输入 `/exit`
614. **When** 退出交互模式
615. **Then** 显示 `会话 chat-a3f8b2c1 已保存，输入 /resume 可恢复`
616. 
617. ---
618. 
619. ### Story 37.9: 中文输入修复
620. 
621. As a 中文用户,
622. I want 删除中文字符时按一次 backspace 就删掉整个字,
623. So that 输入体验流畅自然.
624. 
625. **问题根因：** Swift 的 `readLine()` 在某些终端下将 UTF-8 多字节字符的每个字节视为独立的 backspace 事件。
626. 
627. **实施方案：**
628. 
629. 1. 检测终端编码是否为 UTF-8
630. 2. 如果 `readLine()` 行为不正确，使用替代输入方案：
631.    - 方案 A：使用 Swift 的 `FileHandle.standardInput` 直接读取 raw bytes，手动处理 UTF-8 解码和 backspace
632.    - 方案 B：在 REPL 循环中过滤无效的中间状态（删除不完整的 UTF-8 字节序列）
633. 
634. 3. 或采用更简单的方案：检测到不完整的 UTF-8 序列时，补齐删除
635. 
636. ```swift
637. // 过滤 readLine 返回内容中的无效 UTF-8
638. func cleanInput(_ input: String) -> String {
639.     // 如果输入中包含 Unicode replacement character (U+FFFD)，
640.     // 说明有编码问题，尝试修复
641.     return input
642. }
643. ```
644. 
645. **Acceptance Criteria：**
646. 
647. **Given** 用户输入了 `你好世界`
648. **When** 按一次 backspace
649. **Then** 删除 `界`，显示 `你好世`
650. 
651. **Given** 用户输入了 `hello`
652. **When** 按一次 backspace
653. **Then** 删除 `o`，显示 `hell`（英文行为不变）
654. 
655. ---
656. 
657. ## Story 间的依赖关系
658. 
659. ```
660. 37.0 Coding Agent 系统提示 (P0)  ← 其他所有 story 的基础
661.   │
662.   ├──► 37.1 Slash 命令体系 (P0)
663.   │       │
664.   │       ├──► 37.3 启动横幅 (P1)  ← /cost 数据来源
665.   │       │
666.   │       ├──► 37.7 上下文管理 (P1) ← /compact 实现
667.   │       │
668.   │       └──► 37.8 会话恢复 (P1)  ← /resume 列表选择
669.   │
670.   ├──► 37.2 Ctrl+C 中断 (P0)
671.   │
672.   ├──► 37.4 终端输出优化 (P1)
673.   │
674.   ├──► 37.5 权限审批 (P0)
675.   │
676.   ├──► 37.6 多行输入 (P1)
677.   │
678.   └──► 37.9 中文输入修复 (P2)
679. ```
680. 
681. 建议实现顺序：37.0 → 37.1 → 37.2 → 37.5 → 37.3 → 37.4 → 37.6 → 37.7 → 37.8 → 37.9
682. 
683. ---
684. 
685. ## 实现优先级
686. 
687. | Story | 优先级 | 理由 |
688. |-------|--------|------|
689. | 37.0 Coding Agent 系统提示 | P0 | 所有功能基础，当前 prompt 不适合 coding 场景 |
690. | 37.1 Slash 命令体系 | P0 | 交互模式基础设施，/cost、/compact、/sessions 依赖它 |
691. | 37.2 Ctrl+C 中断 | P0 | 基本可用性需求，无中断功能严重影响体验 |
692. | 37.5 权限审批 | P0 | 安全性需求，默认 bypassPermissions 太危险 |
693. | 37.3 启动横幅 | P1 | 信息展示，不影响核心功能 |
694. | 37.4 终端输出优化 | P1 | 体验提升，不影响核心功能 |
695. | 37.6 多行输入 | P1 | 体验提升，单行输入已可用 |
696. | 37.7 上下文管理 | P1 | 长对话场景必需，短对话无影响 |
697. | 37.8 会话恢复 | P1 | 连续工作流需求，新建会话可用 |
698. | 37.9 中文输入修复 | P2 | 影响中文用户，有 workaround（重输） |
699. 
700. ---
701. 
702. ## 关键设计约束
703. 
704. - **不修改 `SDKTerminalOutputHandler`** — 它被 `RunCommand` 使用，Chat 有独立格式化
705. - **复用 SDK 机制** — PermissionMode、SessionStore、compact 已由 SDK 提供
706. - **渐进式** — 每个 story 独立可用，不阻塞其他 story
707. - **TTY 检测** — 非交互环境（管道输入）保持简单 readLine 行为
708. - **向后兼容** — `axion run "task"` 行为完全不受影响
709. - **独立 System Prompt** — Chat 模式的 prompt 与 Run 模式完全隔离，互不影响
710. - **参数从 BuildConfig 传递** — 上下文窗口、maxTokens、compressionThreshold 等在 BuildConfig 中统一配置
711. 
712. ## 现有代码参考
713. 
714. | 文件 | 说明 |
715. |------|------|
716. | `Sources/AxionCLI/Commands/ChatCommand.swift` | MVP 实现，~97 行 |
717. | `Sources/AxionCLI/Commands/ResumeCommand.swift` | 现有 resume 实现（走 AxionRuntime） |
718. | `Sources/AxionCLI/Commands/SDKOutputHandlers.swift` | 现有输出处理，Chat 模式不直接使用 |
719. | `Sources/AxionCLI/Services/AgentBuilder.swift` | BuildConfig.forCLI() 构建配置 |
720. | `Sources/AxionCLI/AxionCLI.swift` | defaultSubcommand 注册 |
721. | `Resources/prompts/planner-system.md` | 现有桌面自动化 system prompt |
722. 
723. ## 测试策略
724. 
725. - **单元测试** — SlashCommand.parse()、MarkdownTerminalRenderer、权限判断逻辑、CLAUDE.md 加载
726. - **集成测试** — 管道输入模拟多轮对话（`printf` 方式，已在 MVP 验证中使用）
727. - **手动测试** — TTY 交互场景（中文输入、Ctrl+C、粘贴、多行）
728. - **回归测试** — 确保 `axion run "task"` 行为不受影响
729. - **System Prompt 测试** — 验证 coding 模式下 agent 不使用桌面自动化指令
730.
````

</details>

1. use strum::IntoEnumIterator;
2. use strum_macros::AsRefStr;
3. use strum_macros::EnumIter;
4. use strum_macros::EnumString;
5. use strum_macros::IntoStaticStr;
6. 
7. /// Commands that can be invoked by starting a message with a leading slash.
8. #[derive(
9.     Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, EnumString, EnumIter, AsRefStr, IntoStaticStr,
10. )]
11. #[strum(serialize_all = "kebab-case")]
12. pub enum SlashCommand {
13.     // DO NOT ALPHA-SORT! Enum order is presentation order in the popup, so
14.     // more frequently used commands should be listed first.
15.     Model,
16.     Ide,
17.     Permissions,
18.     Keymap,
19.     Vim,
20.     #[strum(serialize = "setup-default-sandbox")]
21.     ElevateSandbox,
22.     #[strum(serialize = "sandbox-add-read-dir")]
23.     SandboxReadRoot,
24.     Experimental,
25.     #[strum(to_string = "approve")]
26.     AutoReview,
27.     Memories,
28.     Skills,
29.     Hooks,
30.     Review,
31.     Rename,
32.     New,
33.     Archive,
34.     Resume,
35.     Fork,
36.     App,
37.     Init,
38.     Compact,
39.     Plan,
40.     Goal,
41.     Agent,
42.     Side,
43.     Btw,
44.     Copy,
45.     Raw,
46.     Diff,
47.     Mention,
48.     Status,
49.     DebugConfig,
50.     Title,
51.     Statusline,
52.     Theme,
53.     #[strum(to_string = "pets", serialize = "pet")]
54.     Pets,
55.     Mcp,
56.     Apps,
57.     Plugins,
58.     Logout,
59.     Quit,
60.     Exit,
61.     Feedback,
62.     Rollout,
63.     Ps,
64.     #[strum(to_string = "stop", serialize = "clean")]
65.     Stop,
66.     Clear,
67.     Personality,
68.     Realtime,
69.     Settings,
70.     TestApproval,
71.     #[strum(serialize = "subagents")]
72.     MultiAgents,
73.     // Debugging commands.
74.     #[strum(serialize = "debug-m-drop")]
75.     MemoryDrop,
76.     #[strum(serialize = "debug-m-update")]
77.     MemoryUpdate,
78. }
79. 
80. impl SlashCommand {
81.     /// User-visible description shown in the popup.
82.     pub fn description(self) -> &'static str {
83.         match self {
84.             SlashCommand::Feedback => "send logs to maintainers",
85.             SlashCommand::New => "start a new chat during a conversation",
86.             SlashCommand::Init => "create an AGENTS.md file with instructions for Codex",
87.             SlashCommand::Compact => "summarize conversation to prevent hitting the context limit",
88.             SlashCommand::Review => "review my current changes and find issues",
89.             SlashCommand::Rename => "rename the current thread",
90.             SlashCommand::Resume => "resume a saved chat",
91.             SlashCommand::Archive => "archive this session and exit",
92.             SlashCommand::Clear => "clear the terminal and start a new chat",
93.             SlashCommand::Fork => "fork the current chat",
94.             SlashCommand::App => "continue this session in Codex Desktop",
95.             SlashCommand::Quit | SlashCommand::Exit => "exit Codex",
96.             SlashCommand::Copy => "copy last response as markdown",
97.             SlashCommand::Raw => "toggle raw scrollback mode for copy-friendly terminal selection",
98.             SlashCommand::Diff => "show git diff (including untracked files)",
99.             SlashCommand::Mention => "mention a file",
100.             SlashCommand::Skills => "use skills to improve how Codex performs specific tasks",
101.             SlashCommand::Hooks => "view and manage lifecycle hooks",
102.             SlashCommand::Status => "show current session configuration and token usage",
103.             SlashCommand::DebugConfig => "show config layers and requirement sources for debugging",
104.             SlashCommand::Title => "configure which items appear in the terminal title",
105.             SlashCommand::Statusline => "configure which items appear in the status line",
106.             SlashCommand::Theme => "choose a syntax highlighting theme",
107.             SlashCommand::Pets => "choose or hide the terminal pet",
108.             SlashCommand::Ps => "list background terminals",
109.             SlashCommand::Stop => "stop all background terminals",
110.             SlashCommand::MemoryDrop => "DO NOT USE",
111.             SlashCommand::MemoryUpdate => "DO NOT USE",
112.             SlashCommand::Model => "choose what model and reasoning effort to use",
113.             SlashCommand::Ide => {
114.                 "include current selection, open files, and other context from your IDE"
115.             }
116.             SlashCommand::Personality => "choose a communication style for Codex",
117.             SlashCommand::Realtime => "toggle realtime voice mode (experimental)",
118.             SlashCommand::Settings => "configure realtime microphone/speaker",
119.             SlashCommand::Plan => "switch to Plan mode",
120.             SlashCommand::Goal => "set or view the goal for a long-running task",
121.             SlashCommand::Agent | SlashCommand::MultiAgents => "switch the active agent thread",
122.             SlashCommand::Side | SlashCommand::Btw => {
123.                 "start a side conversation in an ephemeral fork"
124.             }
125.             SlashCommand::Permissions => "choose what Codex is allowed to do",
126.             SlashCommand::Keymap => "remap TUI shortcuts",
127.             SlashCommand::Vim => "toggle Vim mode for the composer",
128.             SlashCommand::ElevateSandbox => "set up elevated agent sandbox",
129.             SlashCommand::SandboxReadRoot => {
130.                 "let sandbox read a directory: /sandbox-add-read-dir <absolute_path>"
131.             }
132.             SlashCommand::Experimental => "toggle experimental features",
133.             SlashCommand::AutoReview => "approve one retry of a recent auto-review denial",
134.             SlashCommand::Memories => "configure memory use and generation",
135.             SlashCommand::Mcp => "list configured MCP tools; use /mcp verbose for details",
136.             SlashCommand::Apps => "manage apps",
137.             SlashCommand::Plugins => "browse plugins",
138.             SlashCommand::Logout => "log out of Codex",
139.             SlashCommand::Rollout => "print the rollout file path",
140.             SlashCommand::TestApproval => "test approval request",
141.         }
142.     }
143. 
144.     /// Command string without the leading '/'. Provided for compatibility with
145.     /// existing code that expects a method named `command()`.
146.     pub fn command(self) -> &'static str {
147.         self.into()
148.     }
149. 
150.     /// Whether this command supports inline args (for example `/review ...`).
151.     pub fn supports_inline_args(self) -> bool {
152.         matches!(
153.             self,
154.             SlashCommand::Review
155.                 | SlashCommand::Rename
156.                 | SlashCommand::Plan
157.                 | SlashCommand::Goal
158.                 | SlashCommand::Ide
159.                 | SlashCommand::Keymap
160.                 | SlashCommand::Mcp
161.                 | SlashCommand::Raw
162.                 | SlashCommand::Pets
163.                 | SlashCommand::Side
164.                 | SlashCommand::Btw
165.                 | SlashCommand::Resume
166.                 | SlashCommand::SandboxReadRoot
167.         )
168.     }
169. 
170.     /// Whether this command remains available inside an active side conversation.
171.     pub fn available_in_side_conversation(self) -> bool {
172.         matches!(
173.             self,
174.             SlashCommand::Copy
175.                 | SlashCommand::Raw
176.                 | SlashCommand::Diff
177.                 | SlashCommand::Mention
178.                 | SlashCommand::Status
179.                 | SlashCommand::Ide
180.         )
181.     }
182. 
183.     /// Whether this command can be run while a task is in progress.
184.     pub fn available_during_task(self) -> bool {
185.         match self {
186.             SlashCommand::New
187.             | SlashCommand::Archive
188.             | SlashCommand::Resume
189.             | SlashCommand::Fork
190.             | SlashCommand::Init
191.             | SlashCommand::Compact
192.             | SlashCommand::Model
193.             | SlashCommand::Personality
194.             | SlashCommand::Permissions
195.             | SlashCommand::Keymap
196.             | SlashCommand::Vim
197.             | SlashCommand::ElevateSandbox
198.             | SlashCommand::SandboxReadRoot
199.             | SlashCommand::Experimental
200.             | SlashCommand::Memories
201.             | SlashCommand::Review
202.             | SlashCommand::Plan
203.             | SlashCommand::Clear
204.             | SlashCommand::Logout
205.             | SlashCommand::MemoryDrop
206.             | SlashCommand::MemoryUpdate => false,
207.             SlashCommand::Diff
208.             | SlashCommand::Copy
209.             | SlashCommand::Raw
210.             | SlashCommand::Rename
211.             | SlashCommand::Mention
212.             | SlashCommand::Skills
213.             | SlashCommand::Hooks
214.             | SlashCommand::Status
215.             | SlashCommand::DebugConfig
216.             | SlashCommand::Ps
217.             | SlashCommand::Stop
218.             | SlashCommand::App
219.             | SlashCommand::Goal
220.             | SlashCommand::Mcp
221.             | SlashCommand::Apps
222.             | SlashCommand::Plugins
223.             | SlashCommand::Title
224.             | SlashCommand::Statusline
225.             | SlashCommand::AutoReview
226.             | SlashCommand::Feedback
227.             | SlashCommand::Ide
228.             | SlashCommand::Quit
229.             | SlashCommand::Exit
230.             | SlashCommand::Side
231.             | SlashCommand::Btw => true,
232.             SlashCommand::Rollout => true,
233.             SlashCommand::TestApproval => true,
234.             SlashCommand::Realtime => true,
235.             SlashCommand::Settings => true,
236.             SlashCommand::Agent | SlashCommand::MultiAgents => true,
237.             SlashCommand::Theme | SlashCommand::Pets => false,
238.         }
239.     }
240. 
241.     fn is_visible(self) -> bool {
242.         match self {
243.             SlashCommand::SandboxReadRoot => cfg!(target_os = "windows"),
244.             SlashCommand::Copy => !cfg!(target_os = "android"),
245.             SlashCommand::App => cfg!(any(target_os = "macos", target_os = "windows")),
246.             SlashCommand::Rollout | SlashCommand::TestApproval => cfg!(debug_assertions),
247.             _ => true,
248.         }
249.     }
250. }
251. 
252. /// Return all built-in commands in a Vec paired with their command string.
253. pub fn built_in_slash_commands() -> Vec<(&'static str, SlashCommand)> {
254.     SlashCommand::iter()
255.         .filter(|command| command.is_visible())
256.         .map(|c| (c.command(), c))
257.         .collect()
258. }
259. 
260. #[cfg(test)]
```

```
1. //! Shared helpers for filtering and matching built-in and model service-tier slash commands.
2. //!
3. //! The same sandbox- and feature-gating rules are used by both the composer
4. //! and the command popup. Centralizing them here keeps those call sites small
5. //! and ensures they stay in sync.
6. use std::str::FromStr;
7. 
8. use codex_utils_fuzzy_match::fuzzy_match;
9. 
10. use crate::slash_command::SlashCommand;
11. use crate::slash_command::built_in_slash_commands;
12. 
13. #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]
14. pub(crate) struct ServiceTierCommand {
15.     pub(crate) id: String,
16.     pub(crate) name: String,
17.     pub(crate) description: String,
18. }
19. 
20. #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]
21. pub(crate) enum SlashCommandItem {
22.     Builtin(SlashCommand),
23.     ServiceTier(ServiceTierCommand),
24. }
25. 
26. impl SlashCommandItem {
27.     pub(crate) fn command(&self) -> &str {
28.         match self {
29.             Self::Builtin(cmd) => cmd.command(),
30.             Self::ServiceTier(command) => &command.name,
31.         }
32.     }
33. 
34.     pub(crate) fn supports_inline_args(&self) -> bool {
35.         match self {
36.             Self::Builtin(cmd) => cmd.supports_inline_args(),
37.             Self::ServiceTier(_) => false,
38.         }
39.     }
40. 
41.     pub(crate) fn available_in_side_conversation(&self) -> bool {
42.         match self {
43.             Self::Builtin(cmd) => cmd.available_in_side_conversation(),
44.             Self::ServiceTier(_) => false,
45.         }
46.     }
47. 
48.     pub(crate) fn available_during_task(&self) -> bool {
49.         match self {
50.             Self::Builtin(cmd) => cmd.available_during_task(),
51.             Self::ServiceTier(_) => false,
52.         }
53.     }
54. }
55. 
56. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Default)]
57. pub(crate) struct BuiltinCommandFlags {
58.     pub(crate) collaboration_modes_enabled: bool,
59.     pub(crate) connectors_enabled: bool,
60.     pub(crate) plugins_command_enabled: bool,
61.     pub(crate) service_tier_commands_enabled: bool,
62.     pub(crate) goal_command_enabled: bool,
63.     pub(crate) personality_command_enabled: bool,
64.     pub(crate) realtime_conversation_enabled: bool,
65.     pub(crate) audio_device_selection_enabled: bool,
66.     pub(crate) allow_elevate_sandbox: bool,
67.     pub(crate) side_conversation_active: bool,
68. }
69. 
70. /// Return the built-ins that should be visible/usable for the current input.
71. pub(crate) fn builtins_for_input(flags: BuiltinCommandFlags) -> Vec<(&'static str, SlashCommand)> {
72.     built_in_slash_commands()
73.         .into_iter()
74.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.allow_elevate_sandbox || *cmd != SlashCommand::ElevateSandbox)
75.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.collaboration_modes_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Plan)
76.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.connectors_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Apps)
77.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.plugins_command_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Plugins)
78.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.goal_command_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Goal)
79.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.personality_command_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Personality)
80.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.realtime_conversation_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Realtime)
81.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| flags.audio_device_selection_enabled || *cmd != SlashCommand::Settings)
82.         .filter(|(_, cmd)| !flags.side_conversation_active || cmd.available_in_side_conversation())
83.         .collect()
84. }
85. 
86. pub(crate) fn commands_for_input(
87.     flags: BuiltinCommandFlags,
88.     service_tier_commands: &[ServiceTierCommand],
89. ) -> Vec<SlashCommandItem> {
90.     let mut commands = Vec::new();
91.     let tiers_enabled = flags.service_tier_commands_enabled;
92.     for (_, cmd) in builtins_for_input(flags) {
93.         commands.push(SlashCommandItem::Builtin(cmd));
94.         if cmd == SlashCommand::Model && tiers_enabled {
95.             commands.extend(
96.                 service_tier_commands
97.                     .iter()
98.                     .cloned()
99.                     .map(SlashCommandItem::ServiceTier),
100.             );
101.         }
102.     }
103.     commands
104.         .into_iter()
105.         .filter(|cmd| !flags.side_conversation_active || cmd.available_in_side_conversation())
106.         .collect()
107. }
108. 
109. /// Find a single built-in command by exact name, after applying feature gating.
110. ///
111. /// Side-conversation gating is intentionally enforced by dispatch rather than exact lookup so a
112. /// typed command can produce a side-specific unavailable message while the popup still hides it.
113. pub(crate) fn find_builtin_command(name: &str, flags: BuiltinCommandFlags) -> Option<SlashCommand> {
114.     let cmd = SlashCommand::from_str(name).ok()?;
115.     builtins_for_input(BuiltinCommandFlags {
116.         side_conversation_active: false,
117.         ..flags
118.     })
119.     .into_iter()
120.     .any(|(_, visible_cmd)| visible_cmd == cmd)
121.     .then_some(cmd)
122. }
123. 
124. pub(crate) fn find_slash_command(
125.     name: &str,
126.     flags: BuiltinCommandFlags,
127.     service_tier_commands: &[ServiceTierCommand],
128. ) -> Option<SlashCommandItem> {
129.     if let Some(cmd) = find_builtin_command(name, flags) {
130.         return Some(SlashCommandItem::Builtin(cmd));
131.     }
132. 
133.     let tiers_enabled = flags.service_tier_commands_enabled;
134.     tiers_enabled
135.         .then(|| {
136.             service_tier_commands
137.                 .iter()
138.                 .find(|command| command.name == name)
139.                 .cloned()
140.                 .map(SlashCommandItem::ServiceTier)
141.         })
142.         .flatten()
143. }
144. 
145. pub(crate) fn has_slash_command_prefix(
146.     name: &str,
147.     flags: BuiltinCommandFlags,
148.     service_tier_commands: &[ServiceTierCommand],
149. ) -> bool {
150.     commands_for_input(flags, service_tier_commands)
151.         .into_iter()
152.         .any(|command| fuzzy_match(command.command(), name).is_some())
153. }
154.

75. fn next_add_to_history_event(rx: &mut tokio::sync::mpsc::UnboundedReceiver<AppEvent>) -> String {
76.     loop {
77.         match rx.try_recv() {
78.             Ok(AppEvent::AppendMessageHistoryEntry { text, .. }) => return text,
79.             Ok(_) => continue,
80.             Err(TryRecvError::Empty) => {
81.                 panic!("expected AppendMessageHistoryEntry event but queue was empty")
82.             }
83.             Err(TryRecvError::Disconnected) => {
84.                 panic!("expected AppendMessageHistoryEntry event but channel closed")
85.             }
86.         }
87.     }
88. }

243. async fn queued_empty_bang_shell_reports_help_when_dequeued_and_drains_next_input() {
244.     let (mut chat, mut rx, mut op_rx) = make_chatwidget_manual(/*model_override*/ None).await;
245.     chat.thread_id = Some(ThreadId::new());

256.     let rendered = cells
257.         .iter()
258.         .map(|lines| lines_to_single_string(lines))
259.         .collect::<Vec<_>>()
260.         .join("\n");
```

```
1. //! Key binding primitives and input matching for the TUI.
2. //!
3. //! This module provides `KeyBinding`, the runtime representation of a single
4. //! keybinding (key code + modifier set), along with matching logic that handles
5. //! cross-terminal inconsistencies in how shifted letters and raw C0 control
6. //! characters are reported.
7. //!
8. //! List and picker code should match navigation through these helpers instead
9. //! of comparing `KeyEvent` values directly. The matcher owns compatibility for
10. //! terminals that report control chords as C0 characters, while
11. //! `is_plain_text_key_event` gives searchable pickers a shared boundary between
12. //! text input and navigation commands.
13. //!
14. //! It also supplies rendering helpers that convert bindings into styled
15. //! `ratatui::text::Span` values for UI hint display.
16. 
17. use crossterm::event::KeyCode;
18. use crossterm::event::KeyEvent;
19. use crossterm::event::KeyEventKind;
20. use crossterm::event::KeyModifiers;
21. use ratatui::style::Style;
22. use ratatui::style::Stylize;
23. use ratatui::text::Span;
24. 
25. #[cfg(test)]
26. const ALT_PREFIX: &str = "⌥ + ";
27. #[cfg(all(not(test), target_os = "macos"))]
28. const ALT_PREFIX: &str = "⌥ + ";
29. #[cfg(all(not(test), not(target_os = "macos")))]
30. const ALT_PREFIX: &str = "alt + ";
31. const CTRL_PREFIX: &str = "ctrl + ";
32. const SHIFT_PREFIX: &str = "shift + ";
33. 
34. /// One concrete key event that can trigger a TUI action.
35. ///
36. /// Matching via `is_press` handles exact equality plus compatibility fallbacks
37. /// for terminals that report uppercase letters without SHIFT and Ctrl keys as
38. /// raw C0 control characters. This means a binding defined as `shift-a` will
39. /// match either `Shift+a` or plain `A`, and `ctrl-j` will match raw LF.
40. ///
41. /// This does not model multi-key chords or partial matches; callers that need
42. /// sequences must keep that state outside this type.
43. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, Hash, PartialEq)]
44. pub(crate) struct KeyBinding {
45.     key: KeyCode,
46.     modifiers: KeyModifiers,
47. }
48. 
49. impl KeyBinding {
50.     pub(crate) const fn new(key: KeyCode, modifiers: KeyModifiers) -> Self {
51.         Self { key, modifiers }
52.     }
53. 
54.     pub(crate) fn from_event(event: KeyEvent) -> Self {
55.         let (key, modifiers) = normalize_key_parts(event.code, event.modifiers);
56.         Self { key, modifiers }
57.     }
58. 
59.     pub fn is_press(&self, event: KeyEvent) -> bool {
60.         normalize_key_parts(self.key, self.modifiers)
61.             == normalize_key_parts(event.code, event.modifiers)
62.             && (event.kind == KeyEventKind::Press || event.kind == KeyEventKind::Repeat)
63.     }
64. 
65.     pub(crate) const fn parts(&self) -> (KeyCode, KeyModifiers) {
66.         (self.key, self.modifiers)
67.     }
68. 
69.     pub(crate) fn display_label(&self) -> String {
70.         let modifiers = modifiers_to_string(self.modifiers);
71.         let key = match self.key {
72.             KeyCode::Enter => "enter".to_string(),
73.             KeyCode::Char(' ') => "space".to_string(),
74.             KeyCode::Up => "↑".to_string(),
75.             KeyCode::Down => "↓".to_string(),
76.             KeyCode::Left => "←".to_string(),
77.             KeyCode::Right => "→".to_string(),
78.             KeyCode::PageUp => "pgup".to_string(),
79.             KeyCode::PageDown => "pgdn".to_string(),
80.             _ => self.key.to_string().to_ascii_lowercase(),
81.         };
82.         format!("{modifiers}{key}")
83.     }
84. }
85. 
86. pub(crate) fn normalize_key_parts(
87.     key: KeyCode,
88.     mut modifiers: KeyModifiers,
89. ) -> (KeyCode, KeyModifiers) {
90.     let KeyCode::Char(ch) = key else {
91.         return (key, modifiers);
92.     };
93.     if modifiers.is_empty()
94.         && let Some(ctrl_char) = c0_control_char_to_ctrl_char(ch)
95.     {
96.         return (KeyCode::Char(ctrl_char), KeyModifiers::CONTROL | modifiers);
97.     }
98.     if ch.is_ascii_uppercase() {
99.         modifiers.insert(KeyModifiers::SHIFT);
100.         return (KeyCode::Char(ch.to_ascii_lowercase()), modifiers);
101.     }
102.     (key, modifiers)
103. }
104. 
105. fn c0_control_char_to_ctrl_char(ch: char) -> Option<char> {
106.     let code = u32::from(ch);
107.     match code {
108.         0x00 => Some(' '),
109.         0x01..=0x1a => char::from_u32(code - 0x01 + u32::from('a')),
110.         0x1c..=0x1f => char::from_u32(code - 0x1c + u32::from('4')),
111.         _ => None,
112.     }
113. }
114. 
115. /// Matching helpers for one action's keybinding set.
116. ///
117. /// Implementations are expected to treat the slice as alternatives for one
118. /// action. They should not interpret order as priority for dispatch; order is
119. /// reserved for UI hint selection via `primary_binding`.
120. pub(crate) trait KeyBindingListExt {
121.     /// True when any binding in this set matches `event`.
122.     fn is_pressed(&self, event: KeyEvent) -> bool;
123. }
124. 
125. impl KeyBindingListExt for [KeyBinding] {
126.     fn is_pressed(&self, event: KeyEvent) -> bool {
127.         self.iter().any(|binding| binding.is_press(event))
128.     }
129. }
130. 
131. /// Returns whether an event should be treated as literal text input.
132. ///
133. /// Searchable pickers use this to avoid stealing plain printable characters for
134. /// navigation when the same character might be a valid query. For example, a
135. /// list may bind `j` and `k` for movement, but a searchable list must let
136. /// plain `j` update the query while still allowing `Ctrl+J` to move. Calling
137. /// this after normalizing keybindings would blur that distinction and cause
138. /// printable search input to disappear.
139. pub(crate) fn is_plain_text_key_event(event: KeyEvent) -> bool {
140.     matches!(
141.         event,
142.         KeyEvent {
143.             code: KeyCode::Char(ch),
144.             modifiers,
145.             ..
146.         } if !ch.is_ascii_control()
147.             && !modifiers.contains(KeyModifiers::CONTROL)
148.             && !modifiers.contains(KeyModifiers::ALT)
149.     )
150. }
151. 
152. pub(crate) const fn plain(key: KeyCode) -> KeyBinding {
153.     KeyBinding::new(key, KeyModifiers::NONE)
154. }
155. 
156. pub(crate) const fn alt(key: KeyCode) -> KeyBinding {
157.     KeyBinding::new(key, KeyModifiers::ALT)
158. }
159. 
160. pub(crate) const fn shift(key: KeyCode) -> KeyBinding {
161.     KeyBinding::new(key, KeyModifiers::SHIFT)
162. }
163. 
164. pub(crate) const fn ctrl(key: KeyCode) -> KeyBinding {
165.     KeyBinding::new(key, KeyModifiers::CONTROL)
166. }
167. 
168. pub(crate) const fn ctrl_alt(key: KeyCode) -> KeyBinding {
169.     KeyBinding::new(key, KeyModifiers::CONTROL.union(KeyModifiers::ALT))
170. }
171. 
172. fn modifiers_to_string(modifiers: KeyModifiers) -> String {
173.     let mut result = String::new();
174.     if modifiers.contains(KeyModifiers::CONTROL) {
175.         result.push_str(CTRL_PREFIX);
176.     }
177.     if modifiers.contains(KeyModifiers::SHIFT) {
178.         result.push_str(SHIFT_PREFIX);
179.     }
180.     if modifiers.contains(KeyModifiers::ALT) {
181.         result.push_str(ALT_PREFIX);
182.     }
183.     result
184. }
185. 
186. impl From<KeyBinding> for Span<'static> {
187.     fn from(binding: KeyBinding) -> Self {
188.         (&binding).into()
189.     }
190. }
191. impl From<&KeyBinding> for Span<'static> {
192.     fn from(binding: &KeyBinding) -> Self {
193.         Span::styled(binding.display_label(), key_hint_style())
194.     }
195. }
196. 
197. fn key_hint_style() -> Style {
198.     Style::default().dim()
199. }
200. 
201. pub(crate) fn has_ctrl_or_alt(mods: KeyModifiers) -> bool {
202.     (mods.contains(KeyModifiers::CONTROL) || mods.contains(KeyModifiers::ALT)) && !is_altgr(mods)
203. }
204. 
205. #[cfg(windows)]
206. #[inline]
207. pub(crate) fn is_altgr(mods: KeyModifiers) -> bool {
208.     mods.contains(KeyModifiers::ALT) && mods.contains(KeyModifiers::CONTROL)
209. }
210. 
211. #[cfg(not(windows))]
212. #[inline]
213. pub(crate) fn is_altgr(_mods: KeyModifiers) -> bool {
214.     false
215. }
216. 
217. #[cfg(test)]
218. mod tests {
219.     use super::*;
220. 
221.     #[test]
222.     fn is_press_accepts_press_and_repeat_but_rejects_release() {
223.         let binding = ctrl(KeyCode::Char('k'));
224.         let press = KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('k'), KeyModifiers::CONTROL);
225.         let repeat = KeyEvent {
226.             kind: KeyEventKind::Repeat,
227.             ..press
228.         };
229.         let release = KeyEvent {
230.             kind: KeyEventKind::Release,
231.             ..press
232.         };
233.         let wrong_modifiers = KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('k'), KeyModifiers::NONE);
234. 
235.         assert!(binding.is_press(press));
236.         assert!(binding.is_press(repeat));
237.         assert!(!binding.is_press(release));
238.         assert!(!binding.is_press(wrong_modifiers));
239.     }
240. 
241.     #[test]
242.     fn keybinding_list_ext_matches_any_binding() {
243.         let bindings = [plain(KeyCode::Char('a')), ctrl(KeyCode::Char('b'))];
244. 
245.         assert!(bindings.is_pressed(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('a'), KeyModifiers::NONE)));
246.         assert!(bindings.is_pressed(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('b'), KeyModifiers::CONTROL)));
247.         assert!(!bindings.is_pressed(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('c'), KeyModifiers::NONE)));
248.     }
249. 
250.     #[test]
251.     fn shifted_letter_binding_matches_uppercase_char_events() {
252.         let binding = shift(KeyCode::Char('a'));
253. 
254.         assert!(binding.is_press(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('a'), KeyModifiers::SHIFT)));
255.         assert!(binding.is_press(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('A'), KeyModifiers::NONE)));
256.         assert!(binding.is_press(KeyEvent::new(KeyCode::Char('A'), KeyModifiers::SHIFT)));
257.     }
258.

260.     fn shift_letter_binding_preserves_other_modifiers_with_uppercase_compat() {
```

<details>

```
1. //! Runtime keymap resolution for the TUI.
2. //!
3. //! This module converts deserialized config (`TuiKeymap`) into a concrete
4. //! `RuntimeKeymap` used by input handlers at runtime.
5. //!
6. //! Key responsibilities:
7. //!
8. //! 1. Apply deterministic precedence (`context -> global fallback -> defaults`).
9. //! 2. Parse canonical key spec strings into `KeyBinding` values.
10. //! 3. Enforce uniqueness across runtime surfaces so one key cannot trigger
11. //!    multiple actions on the same focused input path.
12. //! 4. Return actionable, user-facing error messages with config paths and next
13. //!    steps.
14. //!
15. //! Non-responsibilities:
16. //!
17. //! 1. This module does not decide which action should run in a given screen.
18. //!    Callers resolve actions by checking the relevant action binding set.
19. //! 2. This module does not persist configuration; it only resolves loaded config.
20. 
21. use crate::key_hint;
22. use crate::key_hint::KeyBinding;
23. use codex_config::types::KeybindingsSpec;
24. use codex_config::types::MAX_FUNCTION_KEY;
25. use codex_config::types::TuiKeymap;
26. use crossterm::event::KeyCode;
27. use crossterm::event::KeyModifiers;
28. use serde::Serialize;
29. use std::collections::HashMap;
30. 
31. /// Runtime keymap used by TUI input handlers.
32. ///
33. /// Resolution precedence is:
34. ///
35. /// 1. Context-specific binding (`tui.keymap.<context>`).
36. /// 2. `tui.keymap.global` for actions that support global fallback.
37. /// 3. Built-in defaults.
38. ///
39. /// This is the only shape UI code should use for dispatch. It represents a
40. /// fully resolved snapshot with parsing, fallback, explicit unbinding, and
41. /// duplicate-key validation already applied. If a caller keeps using an older
42. /// snapshot after config changes, visible hints and active handlers can drift.
43. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
44. pub(crate) struct RuntimeKeymap {
45.     pub(crate) app: AppKeymap,
46.     pub(crate) chat: ChatKeymap,
47.     pub(crate) composer: ComposerKeymap,
48.     pub(crate) editor: EditorKeymap,
49.     pub(crate) vim_normal: VimNormalKeymap,
50.     pub(crate) vim_operator: VimOperatorKeymap,
51.     pub(crate) vim_text_object: VimTextObjectKeymap,
52.     pub(crate) pager: PagerKeymap,
53.     pub(crate) list: ListKeymap,
54.     pub(crate) approval: ApprovalKeymap,
55. }
56. 
57. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
58. pub(crate) struct AppKeymap {
59.     /// Open transcript overlay.
60.     pub(crate) open_transcript: Vec<KeyBinding>,
61.     /// Open external editor for the current draft.
62.     pub(crate) open_external_editor: Vec<KeyBinding>,
63.     /// Copy the last agent response to the clipboard.
64.     pub(crate) copy: Vec<KeyBinding>,
65.     /// Clear the terminal UI.
66.     pub(crate) clear_terminal: Vec<KeyBinding>,
67.     /// Toggle Vim mode for the composer input.
68.     pub(crate) toggle_vim_mode: Vec<KeyBinding>,
69.     /// Toggle Fast mode.
70.     pub(crate) toggle_fast_mode: Vec<KeyBinding>,
71.     /// Toggle raw scrollback mode for copy-friendly transcript selection.
72.     pub(crate) toggle_raw_output: Vec<KeyBinding>,
73. }
74. 
75. /// Chat-level keybindings evaluated at the app event layer.
76. ///
77. /// These participate in the first app-scope conflict validation pass alongside
78. /// `AppKeymap` actions because both are checked before input reaches the
79. /// composer. Dispatch gating (empty-composer guard for backtrack) happens in
80. /// handler code, not here.
81. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
82. pub(crate) struct ChatKeymap {
83.     /// Interrupt the active turn.
84.     pub(crate) interrupt_turn: Vec<KeyBinding>,
85.     /// Decrease the active reasoning effort.
86.     pub(crate) decrease_reasoning_effort: Vec<KeyBinding>,
87.     /// Increase the active reasoning effort.
88.     pub(crate) increase_reasoning_effort: Vec<KeyBinding>,
89.     /// Edit the most recently queued message.
90.     pub(crate) edit_queued_message: Vec<KeyBinding>,
91. }
92. 
93. /// Composer-level keybindings validated in the second app-scope conflict pass.
94. ///
95. /// App-level handlers execute before the composer receives input, so any key
96. /// bound here that also appears in `AppKeymap` would be silently intercepted.
97. /// The conflict validator prevents this by checking app + composer uniqueness.
98. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
99. pub(crate) struct ComposerKeymap {
100.     /// Submit current draft.
101.     pub(crate) submit: Vec<KeyBinding>,
102.     /// Queue current draft while a task is running.
103.     pub(crate) queue: Vec<KeyBinding>,
104.     /// Toggle composer shortcut overlay.
105.     pub(crate) toggle_shortcuts: Vec<KeyBinding>,
106.     /// Open reverse history search or move to the previous match.
107.     pub(crate) history_search_previous: Vec<KeyBinding>,
108.     /// Move to the next match in reverse history search.
109.     pub(crate) history_search_next: Vec<KeyBinding>,
110. }
111. 
112. /// Editor-specific keybindings used by the composer textarea.
113. ///
114. /// These bindings are interpreted only by text-editing widgets and do not
115. /// participate in global/chat fallback resolution.
116. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]

137. /// Vim normal-mode keybindings for modal editing in the composer textarea.
138. ///
139. /// Normal mode is the resting state when Vim is enabled. Pressing a movement
140. /// or editing key here either moves the cursor, triggers an operator-pending

142. /// to insert mode. Default bindings include both `shift(letter)` and

174. /// Vim operator-pending keybindings active after `d` or `y` in normal mode.
175. ///
176. /// When an operator (`start_delete_operator` or `start_yank_operator`) is
177. /// pressed, the next keypress is matched against this context to determine the
178. /// motion range. Repeating the operator key (`dd`, `yy`) acts on the whole
179. /// line. `Esc` cancels the pending operator and returns to normal mode.

227. /// Generic list picker keybindings shared across popup list views.
228. ///
229. /// These actions describe list intent rather than a specific widget layout.
230. /// Vertical actions move the highlighted row, page and jump actions move within
231. /// the current filtered row set, and horizontal actions are available to views
232. /// that expose adjacent choices such as tabs, toolbar values, or ordered item
233. /// movement. Views that also accept search text are responsible for checking
234. /// `is_plain_text_key_event` before dispatching plain-character bindings so a
235. /// configured `j`, `k`, `h`, or `l` does not steal query input.
236. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
237. pub(crate) struct ListKeymap {
238.     pub(crate) move_up: Vec<KeyBinding>,
239.     pub(crate) move_down: Vec<KeyBinding>,
240.     pub(crate) move_left: Vec<KeyBinding>,
241.     pub(crate) move_right: Vec<KeyBinding>,

243.     pub(crate) page_down: Vec<KeyBinding>,

1. //! The chat composer history module owns shell-style recall and incremental search traversal.
2. //!
3. //! It combines persistent cross-session entries with local in-session entries into one offset
4. //! space. Persistent entries are fetched lazily and re-enter this state machine through
5. //! [`ChatComposerHistory::on_entry_response`], while local entries are already available with full
6. //! draft metadata.
7. //!
8. //! Ctrl+R search is modeled separately from normal Up/Down navigation because it has different
9. //! guarantees: query edits restart from the newest match, repeated Older/Newer keys move through
10. //! unique matching text, pending persistent fetches continue the same scan after the response
11. //! arrives, and boundary hits must not advance hidden cursor state. Search deduplication is scoped
12. //! to a single active search session and uses exact prompt text; it does not mutate stored history
13. //! or change normal history browsing.
14. use std::collections::HashMap;
15. use std::collections::HashSet;
16. use std::path::PathBuf;
17. 
18. use crate::app_event::AppEvent;
19. use crate::app_event_sender::AppEventSender;
20. use crate::bottom_pane::MentionBinding;
21. use crate::mention_codec::decode_history_mentions_with_at_mentions;
22. use codex_protocol::ThreadId;
23. use codex_protocol::user_input::TextElement;
24. 
25. /// A composer history entry that can rehydrate draft state.
26. #[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
27. pub(crate) struct HistoryEntry {
28.     /// Raw text stored in history (may include placeholder strings).
29.     pub(crate) text: String,
30.     /// Text element ranges for placeholders inside `text`.
31.     pub(crate) text_elements: Vec<TextElement>,
32.     /// Local image paths captured alongside `text_elements`.
33.     pub(crate) local_image_paths: Vec<PathBuf>,
34.     /// Remote image URLs restored with this draft.
35.     pub(crate) remote_image_urls: Vec<String>,
36.     /// Mention bindings for tool/app/skill references inside `text`.
37.     pub(crate) mention_bindings: Vec<MentionBinding>,
38.     /// Placeholder-to-payload pairs used to restore large paste content.
39.     pub(crate) pending_pastes: Vec<(String, String)>,
40. }
41. 
42. impl HistoryEntry {
43.     /// Creates a text-only history entry and decodes persisted mention bindings.
44.     ///
45.     /// Persistent history does not store attachment payloads or text-element metadata, so this
46.     /// constructor intentionally leaves those fields empty. Local in-session submissions should be
47.     /// recorded with the full `HistoryEntry` value built by the composer; using `new` for a local
48.     /// image or paste submission would make recall lose placeholder ownership.
49.     pub(crate) fn new(text: String) -> Self {
50.         Self::new_with_at_mentions(text, /*at_mentions_enabled*/ true)
51.     }
52. 
53.     pub(crate) fn new_with_at_mentions(text: String, at_mentions_enabled: bool) -> Self {
54.         let decoded = decode_history_mentions_with_at_mentions(&text, at_mentions_enabled);
55.         Self {
56.             text: decoded.text,
57.             text_elements: Vec::new(),
58.             local_image_paths: Vec::new(),
59.             remote_image_urls: Vec::new(),
60.             mention_bindings: decoded
61.                 .mentions
62.                 .into_iter()
63.                 .map(|mention| MentionBinding {
64.                     sigil: mention.sigil,
65.                     mention: mention.mention,
66.                     path: mention.path,
67.                 })
68.                 .collect(),
69.             pending_pastes: Vec::new(),
70.         }
71.     }
72. 
73.     #[cfg(test)]
74.     pub(crate) fn with_pending(
75.         text: String,
76.         text_elements: Vec<TextElement>,
77.         local_image_paths: Vec<PathBuf>,
78.         pending_pastes: Vec<(String, String)>,
79.     ) -> Self {
80.         Self {
81.             text,
82.             text_elements,
83.             local_image_paths,
84.             remote_image_urls: Vec::new(),
85.             mention_bindings: Vec::new(),
86.             pending_pastes,
87.         }
88.     }
89. 
90.     #[cfg(test)]
91.     pub(crate) fn with_pending_and_remote(

93.         text_elements: Vec<TextElement>,
94.         local_image_paths: Vec<PathBuf>,
95.         pending_pastes: Vec<(String, String)>,
96.         remote_image_urls: Vec<String>,
97.     ) -> Self {
98.         Self {
99.             text,
100.             text_elements,
101.             local_image_paths,
102.             remote_image_urls,
103.             mention_bindings: Vec::new(),
104.             pending_pastes,
105.         }
106.     }
107. }
108. 
109. /// State machine that manages shell-style history navigation (Up/Down) inside
110. /// the chat composer. This struct is intentionally decoupled from the
111. /// rendering widget so the logic remains isolated and easier to test.
112. pub(crate) struct ChatComposerHistory {
113.     /// Thread that owns persistent lookup responses for this metadata snapshot.
114.     thread_id: Option<ThreadId>,
115.     /// Identifier of the persistent history log used for stale lookup rejection.
116.     persistent_log_id: Option<u64>,
117.     /// Number of entries already present in the persistent cross-session
118.     /// history file when the session started.
119.     persistent_entry_count: usize,
120. 
121.     /// Messages submitted by the user *during this UI session* (newest at END).
122.     /// Local entries retain full draft state (text elements, image paths, pending pastes, remote image URLs).
123.     local_history: Vec<HistoryEntry>,
124.     /// Local entries seeded from resumed transcript replay.
125.     replay_seeded_history: Vec<HistoryEntry>,
126. 
127.     /// Cache of persistent history entries fetched on-demand (text-only).
128.     fetched_history: HashMap<usize, HistoryEntry>,
129. 
130.     /// Current cursor within the combined (persistent + local) history. `None`
131.     /// indicates the user is *not* currently browsing history.
132.     history_cursor: Option<isize>,
133.     pending_navigation_direction: Option<HistorySearchDirection>,
134. 
135.     /// The text that was last inserted into the composer as a result of
136.     /// history navigation. Used to decide if further Up/Down presses should be
137.     /// treated as navigation versus normal cursor movement, together with the
138.     /// "cursor at line boundary" check in [`Self::should_handle_navigation`].
139.     last_history_text: Option<String>,
140. 
141.     /// Active incremental history search, if Ctrl+R search mode is open.
142.     search: Option<HistorySearchState>,
143.     /// Whether persistent history restore should rehydrate `@` tool mentions.
144.     at_mention_restore_enabled: bool,
145. }
146. 
147. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq)]
148. pub(crate) enum HistorySearchDirection {
149.     /// Traverse toward older history offsets.
150.     Older,
151.     /// Traverse toward newer history offsets.
152.     Newer,
153. }
154. 
155. /// Result of a single incremental history search step.
156. ///
157. /// `Pending` means a persistent entry lookup has been requested and the caller should keep the
158. /// visible search session open until [`ChatComposerHistory::on_entry_response`] supplies the next
159. /// result. `AtBoundary` means the current selected match is still valid but the requested direction
160. /// has no further unique match; callers should avoid treating it like a query miss.
161. #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq)]
162. pub(crate) enum HistorySearchResult {
163.     Found(HistoryEntry),
164.     Pending,
165.     AtBoundary,
166.     NotFound,
167. }
168. 
169. /// Result of integrating an asynchronous persistent history response.
170. ///
171. /// A response can satisfy normal Up/Down navigation, resume a pending Ctrl+R search scan, or be
172. /// ignored if it belongs to a stale log or an offset the composer no longer needs.
173. #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq)]
174. pub(crate) enum HistoryEntryResponse {
175.     Found(HistoryEntry),
176.     Search(HistorySearchResult),
177.     Ignored,
178. }
179. 
180. /// State for one active Ctrl+R search query.
181. ///
182. /// The state keeps two cursors: `selected_offset` is the raw combined-history offset used to
183. /// continue scanning, while `selected_match_index` points into `unique_matches` so already
184. /// discovered unique results can be revisited without rescanning duplicate offsets. `seen_texts`
185. /// intentionally keys on exact prompt text because the UI previews and accepts text, not the
186. /// storage identity of each historical record.
187. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
188. struct HistorySearchState {
189.     query: String,
190.     query_lower: String,
191.     selected_offset: Option<usize>,
192.     unique_matches: Vec<UniqueHistoryMatch>,
193.     selected_match_index: Option<usize>,
194.     seen_texts: HashSet<String>,
195.     awaiting: Option<PendingHistorySearch>,
196.     exhausted_older: bool,
197.     exhausted_newer: bool,
198. }
199. 
200. /// A unique search match cached with enough draft state to be selected again.
201. ///
202. /// The vector of these matches is kept in newest-to-oldest offset order. Storing the entry beside
203. /// the offset avoids depending on later cache lookups when the user moves Newer/Older among matches
204. /// that have already been discovered.
205. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
206. struct UniqueHistoryMatch {
207.     offset: usize,
208.     entry: HistoryEntry,
209. }
210. 
211. /// Persistent-history lookup currently blocking an incremental search scan.
212. ///
213. /// The pending request records the direction and boundary behavior that were active when the fetch
214. /// was issued so the response can either return a unique match or continue scanning as if no async
215. /// gap had occurred.
216. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug)]
217. struct PendingHistorySearch {
218.     offset: usize,
219.     direction: HistorySearchDirection,
220.     boundary_if_exhausted: bool,
```
