19. 
20. // Hide alias commands in the default popup list so each unique action appears once.
21. // `quit` is an alias of `exit`, and `btw` is an alias of `side`, so we skip
22. // those aliases here.
23. const ALIAS_COMMANDS: &[SlashCommand] = &[SlashCommand::Quit, SlashCommand::Btw];
24. const COMMAND_COLUMN_WIDTH: ColumnWidthConfig = ColumnWidthConfig::new(
25.     ColumnWidthMode::AutoAllRows,
26.     /*name_column_width*/ None,
27. );
28. 
29. /// A selectable item in the popup.
30. #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]
31. pub(crate) enum CommandItem {
32.     Builtin(SlashCommand),
33.     ServiceTier(ServiceTierCommand),
34. }
35. 
36. pub(crate) struct CommandPopup {
37.     command_filter: String,
38.     commands: Vec<CommandItem>,
39.     state: ScrollState,
40. }
41. 
42. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Default)]
43. pub(crate) struct CommandPopupFlags {
44.     pub(crate) collaboration_modes_enabled: bool,
45.     pub(crate) connectors_enabled: bool,
46.     pub(crate) plugins_command_enabled: bool,
47.     pub(crate) service_tier_commands_enabled: bool,
48.     pub(crate) goal_command_enabled: bool,
49.     pub(crate) personality_command_enabled: bool,
50.     pub(crate) realtime_conversation_enabled: bool,
51.     pub(crate) audio_device_selection_enabled: bool,
52.     pub(crate) windows_degraded_sandbox_active: bool,
53.     pub(crate) side_conversation_active: bool,
54. }
55. 
56. impl From<CommandPopupFlags> for BuiltinCommandFlags {
57.     fn from(value: CommandPopupFlags) -> Self {
58.         Self {
59.             collaboration_modes_enabled: value.collaboration_modes_enabled,
60.             connectors_enabled: value.connectors_enabled,
61.             plugins_command_enabled: value.plugins_command_enabled,
62.             service_tier_commands_enabled: value.service_tier_commands_enabled,
63.             goal_command_enabled: value.goal_command_enabled,
64.             personality_command_enabled: value.personality_command_enabled,
65.             realtime_conversation_enabled: value.realtime_conversation_enabled,
66.             audio_device_selection_enabled: value.audio_device_selection_enabled,
67.             allow_elevate_sandbox: value.windows_degraded_sandbox_active,
68.             side_conversation_active: value.side_conversation_active,
69.         }
70.     }
71. }
72. 
73. impl CommandPopup {
74.     pub(crate) fn new(
75.         flags: CommandPopupFlags,
76.         service_tier_commands: Vec<ServiceTierCommand>,
77.     ) -> Self {
78.         // Keep built-in availability in sync with the composer.
79.         let commands = commands_for_input(flags.into(), &service_tier_commands)
80.             .into_iter()
81.             .filter_map(|command| match command {
82.                 SlashCommandItem::Builtin(cmd) => (!cmd.command().starts_with("debug")
83.                     && cmd != SlashCommand::Apps)
84.                     .then_some(CommandItem::Builtin(cmd)),
85.                 SlashCommandItem::ServiceTier(command) => Some(CommandItem::ServiceTier(command)),
86.             })
87.             .collect();
88.         Self {
89.             command_filter: String::new(),
90.             commands,
91.             state: ScrollState::new(),
92.         }
93.     }
94. 
95.     /// Update the filter string based on the current composer text. The text
96.     /// passed in is expected to start with a leading '/'. Everything after the
97.     /// *first* '/' on the *first* line becomes the active filter that is used
98.     /// to narrow down the list of available commands.
99.     pub(crate) fn on_composer_text_change(&mut self, text: String) {
100.         let first_line = text.lines().next().unwrap_or("");
101.         let previous_filter = self.command_filter.clone();
102. 
103.         if let Some(stripped) = first_line.strip_prefix('/') {
104.             // Extract the *first* token (sequence of non-whitespace
105.             // characters) after the slash so that `/clear something` still
106.             // shows the help for `/clear`.
107.             let token = stripped.trim_start();
108.             let cmd_token = token.split_whitespace().next().unwrap_or("");
109. 
110.             // Update the filter keeping the original case (commands are all
111.             // lower-case for now but this may change in the future).
112.             self.command_filter = cmd_token.to_string();
113.         } else {
114.             // The composer no longer starts with '/'. Reset the filter so the
115.             // popup shows the *full* command list if it is still displayed
116.             // for some reason.
117.             self.command_filter.clear();
118.         }
119. 
120.         if self.command_filter != previous_filter {
121.             self.state.reset();
122.         }
123. 
124.         // Reset or clamp selected index based on new filtered list.
125.         let matches_len = self.filtered_items().len();
126.         self.state.clamp_selection(matches_len);
127.         self.state
128.             .ensure_visible(matches_len, MAX_POPUP_ROWS.min(matches_len));
129.     }
130. 
131.     /// Determine the preferred height of the popup for a given width.
132.     /// Accounts for wrapped descriptions so that long tooltips don't overflow.
133.     pub(crate) fn calculate_required_height(&self, width: u16) -> u16 {
134.         let rows = self.rows_from_matches(self.filtered());
135. 
136.         measure_rows_height_with_col_width_mode(
137.             &rows,
138.             &self.state,
139.             MAX_POPUP_ROWS,
140.             width,
141.             COMMAND_COLUMN_WIDTH,
142.         )
143.     }
144. 
145.     /// Compute exact/prefix matches over built-in commands and user prompts,
146.     /// paired with optional highlight indices. Preserves the original
147.     /// presentation order for built-ins and prompts.
148.     fn filtered(&self) -> Vec<(CommandItem, Option<Vec<usize>>)> {
149.         let filter = self.command_filter.trim();
150.         let mut out: Vec<(CommandItem, Option<Vec<usize>>)> = Vec::new();
151.         if filter.is_empty() {
152.             for command in self.commands.iter() {
153.                 if matches!(command, CommandItem::Builtin(cmd) if ALIAS_COMMANDS.contains(cmd)) {
154.                     continue;
155.                 }
156.                 out.push((command.clone(), None));
157.             }
158.             return out;
159.         }
160. 
161.         let filter_lower = filter.to_lowercase();
162.         let filter_chars = filter.chars().count();
163.         let mut exact: Vec<(CommandItem, Option<Vec<usize>>)> = Vec::new();
164.         let mut prefix: Vec<(CommandItem, Option<Vec<usize>>)> = Vec::new();
165.         let indices_for = |offset| Some((offset..offset + filter_chars).collect());
166. 
167.         let mut push_match =
168.             |item: CommandItem, display: &str, name: Option<&str>, name_offset: usize| {
169.                 let display_lower = display.to_lowercase();
170.                 let name_lower = name.map(str::to_lowercase);
171.                 let display_exact = display_lower == filter_lower;
172.                 let name_exact = name_lower.as_deref() == Some(filter_lower.as_str());
173.                 if display_exact || name_exact {
174.                     let offset = if display_exact { 0 } else { name_offset };
175.                     exact.push((item, indices_for(offset)));
176.                     return;
177.                 }
178.                 let display_prefix = display_lower.starts_with(&filter_lower);
179.                 let name_prefix = name_lower
180.                     .as_ref()
181.                     .is_some_and(|name| name.starts_with(&filter_lower));
182.                 if display_prefix || name_prefix {
183.                     let offset = if display_prefix { 0 } else { name_offset };
184.                     prefix.push((item, indices_for(offset)));
185.                 }
186.             };
187. 
188.         for command in self.commands.iter() {
189.             let display = command.command();
190.             push_match(command.clone(), display, None, 0);
191.         }
192. 
193.         out.extend(exact);
194.         out.extend(prefix);
195.         out
196.     }
197. 
198.     fn filtered_items(&self) -> Vec<CommandItem> {
199.         self.filtered().into_iter().map(|(c, _)| c).collect()
200.     }
201. 
202.     fn rows_from_matches(
203.         &self,
204.         matches: Vec<(CommandItem, Option<Vec<usize>>)>,
205.     ) -> Vec<GenericDisplayRow> {
206.         matches
207.             .into_iter()
208.             .map(|(item, indices)| {
209.                 let name = format!("/{}", item.command());
210.                 let description = item.description().to_string();
211.                 GenericDisplayRow {
212.                     name,
213.                     name_prefix_spans: Vec::new(),
214.                     match_indices: indices.map(|v| v.into_iter().map(|i| i + 1).collect()),
215.                     display_shortcut: None,
216.                     description: Some(description),
217.                     category_tag: None,
218.                     wrap_indent: None,
219.                     is_disabled: false,
220.                     disabled_reason: None,
```

</details>

1. //! Composer-side Ctrl+R reverse history search state and rendering helpers.
2. //!
3. //! The persistent and local history stores live in `chat_composer_history`, but the composer owns
4. //! the active search session because it has to snapshot/restore the editable draft, preview matches
5. //! in the textarea, and render the footer prompt while the footer line is acting as the search
6. //! input.
7. //!
8. //! This module is responsible for the UI-facing lifecycle of a search session: recognizing the
9. //! keys that enter and drive search mode, keeping the footer query separate from the textarea
10. //! preview, restoring the original draft on cancellation or misses, and translating history search
11. //! results into composer-visible state. It deliberately does not decide which history entries
12. //! match, how duplicate results are skipped, or when persistent history should be fetched; those
13. //! traversal invariants stay with `ChatComposerHistory`.
14. //!
15. //! A search session starts idle with an empty footer query, so opening Ctrl+R never previews the
16. //! latest history entry by itself. Typing a query restarts traversal from newest to oldest,
17. //! repeated Ctrl+R/Up and Ctrl+S/Down move between unique matches, `Enter` accepts the current
18. //! preview as an editable draft, and `Esc` or Ctrl+C restores the exact draft that existed before
19. //! search started.
20. 
21. use std::ops::Range;
22. 
23. use crossterm::event::KeyCode;
24. use crossterm::event::KeyEvent;
25. use crossterm::event::KeyEventKind;
26. use crossterm::event::KeyModifiers;
27. use ratatui::layout::Constraint;
28. use ratatui::layout::Layout;
29. use ratatui::layout::Rect;
30. use ratatui::style::Stylize;
31. use ratatui::text::Line;
32. use ratatui::text::Span;
33. 
34. use super::super::chat_composer_history::HistorySearchDirection;
35. use super::super::chat_composer_history::HistorySearchResult;
36. use super::super::footer::footer_height;
37. use super::super::footer::reset_mode_after_activity;
38. use super::ActivePopup;
39. use super::ChatComposer;
40. use super::ComposerDraft;
41. use super::InputResult;
42. use crate::app_event::AppEvent;
43. use crate::key_hint;
44. use crate::key_hint::KeyBinding;
45. use crate::key_hint::KeyBindingListExt;
46. use crate::key_hint::has_ctrl_or_alt;
47. use crate::ui_consts::FOOTER_INDENT_COLS;
48. 
49. /// Active composer-owned state for one Ctrl+R search interaction.
50. ///
51. /// The session is created only by [`ChatComposer::begin_history_search`] and is cleared only by
52. /// accepting, canceling, or replacing the search mode. It stores the original draft separately from
53. /// the footer query so transient previews never destroy the user's in-progress composer content.
54. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
55. pub(super) struct HistorySearchSession {
56.     /// Draft to restore when search is canceled or a query has no match.
57.     original_draft: ComposerDraft,
58.     /// Footer-owned query text typed while Ctrl+R search is active.
59.     query: String,
60.     /// User-visible search status used to choose footer hints and composer preview behavior.
61.     status: HistorySearchStatus,
62. }
63. 
64. /// User-visible phase of the active Ctrl+R search session.
65. ///
66. /// Search keeps the footer query and the composer preview separate: `Idle` leaves the original
67. /// draft untouched, `Searching` waits for persistent history, `Match` previews a found entry, and
68. /// `NoMatch` restores the original draft while leaving the search input open for more typing.
69. #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
70. enum HistorySearchStatus {
71.     Idle,
72.     Searching,
73.     Match,
74.     NoMatch,
75. }
76. 
77. impl ChatComposer {
78.     #[cfg(test)]
79.     pub(super) fn history_search_active(&self) -> bool {
80.         self.history_search.is_some()
81.     }
82. 
83.     /// Returns whether a key event should open reverse history search or step to an older match.
84.     ///
85.     /// The check accepts both normal Ctrl+R reports and the raw control character variant that
86.     /// some terminals emit. Callers should only use this before generic text handling; treating the
87.     /// raw control character as ordinary input would insert an invisible byte into the search query
88.     /// or composer draft.
89.     pub(super) fn is_history_search_key(key_event: &KeyEvent, bindings: &[KeyBinding]) -> bool {
90.         bindings.is_pressed(*key_event)
91.     }
92. 
93.     fn is_history_search_forward_key(key_event: &KeyEvent, bindings: &[KeyBinding]) -> bool {
94.         bindings.is_pressed(*key_event)
95.     }
96. 
97.     /// Opens footer-owned reverse history search without previewing history yet.
98.     ///
99.     /// Entering search mode first flushes pending paste-burst text, then snapshots the full
100.     /// composer draft, clears any file/search popup state, and resets history traversal. The first
101.     /// visible match is produced only after the footer query becomes non-empty, which keeps Ctrl+R
102.     /// from replacing an empty composer with the latest prompt before the user has searched for
103.     /// anything.
104.     pub(super) fn begin_history_search(&mut self) -> (InputResult, bool) {
105.         if let Some(pasted) = self.draft.paste_burst.flush_before_modified_input() {
106.             self.handle_paste(pasted);
107.         }
108.         self.draft.paste_burst.clear_window_after_non_char();
109. 
110.         if self.popups.current_file_query.is_some() {
111.             self.app_event_tx
112.                 .send(AppEvent::StartFileSearch(String::new()));
113.             self.popups.current_file_query = None;
114.         }
115.         self.popups.active = ActivePopup::None;
116.         self.attachments.clear_remote_image_selection();
117.         self.history_search = Some(HistorySearchSession {
118.             original_draft: self.snapshot_draft(),
119.             query: String::new(),
120.             status: HistorySearchStatus::Idle,
```

31. /// Resolve the editor command from environment variables.
32. /// Prefers `VISUAL` over `EDITOR`.
33. pub(crate) fn resolve_editor_command() -> std::result::Result<Vec<String>, EditorError> {
34.     let raw = env::var("VISUAL")
35.         .or_else(|_| env::var("EDITOR"))
36.         .map_err(|_| EditorError::MissingEditor)?;
37.     let parts = {
38.         #[cfg(windows)]
39.         {
40.             winsplit::split(&raw)
41.         }
42.         #[cfg(not(windows))]
43.         {
44.             shlex::split(&raw).ok_or(EditorError::ParseFailed)?
45.         }
46.     };
47.     if parts.is_empty() {
48.         return Err(EditorError::EmptyCommand);
49.     }
50.     Ok(parts)
51. }
52. 
53. /// Write `seed` to a temp file, launch the editor command, and return the updated content.
54. pub(crate) async fn run_editor(seed: &str, editor_cmd: &[String]) -> Result<String> {
55.     if editor_cmd.is_empty() {
56.         return Err(Report::msg("editor command is empty"));
57.     }
58. 
59.     // Convert to TempPath immediately so no file handle stays open on Windows.
60.     let temp_path = Builder::new().suffix(".md").tempfile()?.into_temp_path();
61.     fs::write(&temp_path, seed)?;
62. 
63.     let mut cmd = {
64.         #[cfg(windows)]
65.         {
66.             // handles .cmd/.bat shims
67.             Command::new(resolve_windows_program(&editor_cmd[0]))
68.         }
69.         #[cfg(not(windows))]
70.         {
71.             Command::new(&editor_cmd[0])
72.         }
73.     };
74.     if editor_cmd.len() > 1 {
75.         cmd.args(&editor_cmd[1..]);
76.     }
77.     let status = cmd
78.         .arg(&temp_path)
79.         .stdin(Stdio::inherit())
80.         .stdout(Stdio::inherit())
81.         .stderr(Stdio::inherit())
82.         .status()
83.         .await?;
84. 
85.     if !status.success() {
86.         return Err(Report::msg(format!("editor exited with status {status}")));
87.     }
88. 
89.     let contents = fs::read_to_string(&temp_path)?;
90.     Ok(contents)
91. }
92. 
93. #[cfg(test)]
94. mod tests {
95.     use super::*;
```

16. /// Visual state for the file-search popup.
17. pub(crate) struct FileSearchPopup {
18.     /// Query corresponding to the `matches` currently shown.
19.     display_query: String,
20.     /// Latest query typed by the user. May differ from `display_query` when
21.     /// a search is still in-flight.
22.     pending_query: String,
23.     /// When `true` we are still waiting for results for `pending_query`.
24.     waiting: bool,
25.     /// Cached matches; paths relative to the search dir.
26.     matches: Vec<FileMatch>,
27.     /// Shared selection/scroll state.
28.     state: ScrollState,
29. }
30. 
31. impl FileSearchPopup {
32.     pub(crate) fn new() -> Self {
33.         Self {
34.             display_query: String::new(),
35.             pending_query: String::new(),
36.             waiting: true,
37.             matches: Vec::new(),
38.             state: ScrollState::new(),
39.         }
40.     }
41. 
42.     /// Update the query and reset state to *waiting*.
43.     pub(crate) fn set_query(&mut self, query: &str) {
44.         if query == self.pending_query {
45.             return;
46.         }
47. 
48.         self.pending_query.clear();
49.         self.pending_query.push_str(query);
50. 
51.         self.waiting = true; // waiting for new results
52.     }
53. 
54.     /// Put the popup into an "idle" state used for an empty query (just "@").
55.     /// Shows a hint instead of matches until the user types more characters.
56.     pub(crate) fn set_empty_prompt(&mut self) {
57.         self.display_query.clear();
58.         self.pending_query.clear();
59.         self.waiting = false;
60.         self.matches.clear();
61.         // Reset selection/scroll state when showing the empty prompt.
62.         self.state.reset();
63.     }
64. 
65.     /// Replace matches when a `FileSearchResult` arrives.
66.     /// Replace matches. Only applied when `query` matches `pending_query`.
67.     pub(crate) fn set_matches(&mut self, query: &str, matches: Vec<FileMatch>) {
68.         if query != self.pending_query {
69.             return; // stale
70.         }
71. 
72.         self.display_query = query.to_string();
73.         self.matches = matches.into_iter().take(MAX_POPUP_ROWS).collect();
74.         self.waiting = false;
75.         let len = self.matches.len();
76.         self.state.clamp_selection(len);
77.         self.state.ensure_visible(len, len.min(MAX_POPUP_ROWS));
78.     }
79. 
80.     /// Move selection cursor up.
81.     pub(crate) fn move_up(&mut self) {
82.         let len = self.matches.len();
83.         self.state.move_up_wrap(len);
84.         self.state.ensure_visible(len, len.min(MAX_POPUP_ROWS));
85.     }
86. 
87.     /// Move selection cursor down.
88.     pub(crate) fn move_down(&mut self) {
89.         let len = self.matches.len();
90.         self.state.move_down_wrap(len);
91.         self.state.ensure_visible(len, len.min(MAX_POPUP_ROWS));
92.     }
93. 
94.     pub(crate) fn selected_match(&self) -> Option<&PathBuf> {
95.         self.state
96.             .selected_idx
97.             .and_then(|idx| self.matches.get(idx))
98.             .map(|file_match| &file_match.path)
99.     }
100. 
101.     pub(crate) fn calculate_required_height(&self) -> u16 {
102.         // Row count depends on whether we already have matches. If no matches
103.         // yet (e.g. initial search or query with no results) reserve a single
104.         // row so the popup is still visible. When matches are present we show
105.         // up to MAX_RESULTS regardless of the waiting flag so the list
106.         // remains stable while a newer search is in-flight.
107. 
108.         self.matches.len().clamp(1, MAX_POPUP_ROWS) as u16
109.     }
110. }

```
1. //! Transient side-conversation threads.
2. //!
3. //! A side conversation is an ephemeral fork used for a quick /side question while keeping the
4. //! primary thread focused. This module owns the app-level lifecycle for those forks: switching into
5. //! them, returning to their parent, and discarding them when normal thread navigation moves
6. //! elsewhere. The fork receives hidden developer instructions that make inherited history reference
7. //! material only and steer the agent away from mutations unless the side conversation explicitly asks
8. //! for them.
9. 
10. use super::*;
11. use crate::chatwidget::InterruptedTurnNoticeMode;
12. use codex_protocol::models::ContentItem;
13. use codex_protocol::models::ResponseItem;
14. 
15. const SIDE_RENAME_BLOCK_MESSAGE: &str = "Side conversations are ephemeral and cannot be renamed.";
16. const SIDE_MAIN_THREAD_UNAVAILABLE_MESSAGE: &str =
17.     "'/side' is unavailable until the main thread is ready.";
18. const SIDE_NO_STARTED_CONVERSATION_MESSAGE: &str = concat!(
19.     "'/side' is unavailable until the current conversation has started. ",

49. 
50. #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, PartialEq, Eq)]
51. pub(super) enum SideParentStatus {
52.     NeedsInput,
53.     NeedsApproval,
54.     Failed,
55.     Interrupted,
56.     Closed,
57.     Finished,
58. }
59.

61.     fn label(self, parent_is_main: bool) -> &'static str {
62.         match (self, parent_is_main) {
63.             (SideParentStatus::NeedsInput, true) => "main needs input",
64.             (SideParentStatus::NeedsInput, false) => "parent needs input",
65.             (SideParentStatus::NeedsApproval, true) => "main needs approval",
66.             (SideParentStatus::NeedsApproval, false) => "parent needs approval",
67.             (SideParentStatus::Failed, true) => "main failed",
68.             (SideParentStatus::Failed, false) => "parent failed",
69.             (SideParentStatus::Interrupted, true) => "main interrupted",
70.             (SideParentStatus::Interrupted, false) => "parent interrupted",

**view the file at /Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/SlashCommand.swift.**

```
1. import Foundation
2. 
3. /// 斜杠命令枚举。不依赖 SDK 类型，纯解析层。
4. ///
5. /// 注意：`/quit` 在 parse() 中映射为 `.exit`，不出现在 allCases 中
6. /// （allCases 用于 /help 输出，/quit 是 /exit 的别名）。
7. enum SlashCommand: String, CaseIterable, Equatable {
8.     case help = "/help"
9.     case clear = "/clear"
10.     case compact = "/compact"
11.     case model = "/model"     // 带可选参数
12.     case cost = "/cost"
13.     case resume = "/resume"
14.     case config = "/config"
15.     case exit = "/exit"
16. 
17.     /// 解析用户输入为 SlashCommand。非斜杠命令或未知命令返回 nil。
18.     static func parse(_ input: String) -> SlashCommand? {
19.         let trimmed = input.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
20.         guard trimmed.hasPrefix("/") else { return nil }
21.         let parts = trimmed.split(separator: " ", maxSplits: 1)
22.         let cmd = String(parts[0]).lowercased()
23.         switch cmd {
24.         case "/help":    return .help
25.         case "/clear":   return .clear
26.         case "/compact": return .compact
27.         case "/model":   return .model
28.         case "/cost":    return .cost
29.         case "/resume":  return .resume
30.         case "/config":  return .config
31.         case "/exit", "/quit": return .exit
32.         default: return nil
33.         }
34.     }
35. 
36.     /// 提取命令参数（命令名之后的部分，已 trim）。
37.     static func parseArgument(_ input: String) -> String? {
38.         let parts = input.split(separator: " ", maxSplits: 1)
39.         guard parts.count > 1 else { return nil }
40.         let arg = String(parts[1]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
41.         return arg.isEmpty ? nil : arg
42.     }
43. 
44.     /// 用于 /help 显示的简短描述。
45.     var helpText: String {
46.         switch self {
47.         case .help:    return "显示帮助信息"
48.         case .clear:   return "清屏（不重置会话）"
49.         case .compact: return "压缩上下文"
50.         case .model:   return "显示/切换模型（/model [name]）"
51.         case .cost:    return "显示当前会话 token 用量和成本"
52.         case .resume:  return "恢复会话（/resume [id]）"
53.         case .config:  return "显示当前配置"
54.         case .exit:    return "退出交互模式（/quit 同义）"
55.         }
56.     }
57. }
58.
```

/Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/SlashCommandHandler.swift (lines 1-220)

```
1. import AxionCore
2. import Foundation
3. import OpenAgentSDK
4. 
5. /// SlashCommandHandler.handle() 的返回类型。
6. ///
7. /// 支持 REPL 循环根据不同 action 执行不同的后续逻辑。
8. enum SlashCommandAction: Equatable, Sendable {
9.     case none              // 继续循环
10.     case exit              // 退出 REPL
11.     case resumeSession(String)  // 恢复指定 session
12. }
13. 
14. /// 处理 REPL 斜杠命令的具体逻辑。
15. ///
16. /// 所有方法为 `static`，不持有状态。`Agent` 等引用通过参数传入。
17. struct SlashCommandHandler {
18. 
19.     // MARK: - Cost estimation constants
20. 
21.     /// Anthropic 公开定价（美元/百万 token），简化估算。
22.     private static let sonnetInputCostPerMTokens: Double = 3.0
23.     private static let sonnetOutputCostPerMTokens: Double = 15.0
24.     private static let sonnetCacheReadCostPerMTokens: Double = 0.30
25.     private static let opusInputCostPerMTokens: Double = 15.0
26.     private static let opusOutputCostPerMTokens: Double = 75.0
27.     private static let opusCacheReadCostPerMTokens: Double = 1.50
28. 
29.     // MARK: - Public entry point
30. 
31.     /// 处理 slash 命令。返回 action 指示 REPL 循环的后续行为。
32.     static func handle(
33.         _ command: SlashCommand,
34.         argument: String?,
35.         agent: Agent,
36.         config: AxionConfig,
37.         sessionUsage: TokenUsage,
38.         buildConfig: AgentBuilder.BuildConfig,
39.         contextWindow: Int = 0,
40.         contextTokens: Int = 0
41.     ) -> SlashCommandAction {
42.         switch command {
43.         case .help:
44.             fputs(handleHelp(), stderr)
45.         case .clear:
46.             handleClear()
47.         case .compact:
48.             fputs(handleCompact(contextTokens: contextTokens, contextWindow: contextWindow), stderr)
49.         case .model:
50.             handleModel(argument: argument, agent: agent)
51.         case .cost:
52.             fputs(handleCost(usage: sessionUsage, model: agent.model, contextTokens: contextTokens, contextWindow: contextWindow), stderr)
53.         case .resume:
54.             return handleResume(argument: argument)
55.         case .config:
56.             fputs(
57.                 handleConfig(
58.                     model: agent.model,
59.                     maxTokens: buildConfig.maxTokens ?? 4096,
60.                     maxSteps: buildConfig.maxSteps ?? config.maxSteps,
61.                     noMemory: buildConfig.noMemory,
62.                     noSkills: buildConfig.noSkills,
63.                     permissionMode: PermissionHandler.modeDisplayName(buildConfig.permissionMode)
64.                 ),
65.                 stderr
66.             )
67.         case .exit:
68.             return .exit
69.         }
70.         return .none
71.     }
72. 
73.     // MARK: - Individual handlers
74. 
75.     /// /help — 格式化输出所有命令列表。
76.     static func handleHelp() -> String {
77.         var lines = ["可用命令:\n"]
78.         for cmd in SlashCommand.allCases {
79.             lines.append("  \(cmd.rawValue.padding(toLength: 10, withPad: " ", startingAt: 0)) \(cmd.helpText)")
80.         }
81.         lines.append("\n  /quit                 退出交互模式（/exit 同义）")
82.         return lines.joined(separator: "\n") + "\n"
83.     }
84. 
85.     /// /clear — ANSI escape 清屏。
86.     static func handleClear() {
87.         fputs("\u{1B}[2J\u{1B}[H", stdout)
88.         fflush(stdout)
89.     }
90. 
91.     /// /model — 生成显示当前模型名称的文本（无参数时）。
92.     static func handleModelDisplay(model: String) -> String {
93.         "当前模型: \(model)\n"
94.     }
95. 
96.     /// /model — 生成切换模型成功的确认文本。
97.     static func handleModelSwitchSuccess(_ modelName: String) -> String {
98.         "[axion] 模型已切换为 \(modelName)\n"
99.     }
100. 
101.     /// /model — 生成切换失败的错误文本。
102.     static func handleModelSwitchError(_ error: Error) -> String {
103.         "[axion] 切换失败: \(error.localizedDescription)\n"
104.     }
105. 
106.     /// /model — 显示当前模型或切换模型。
107.     static func handleModel(argument: String?, agent: Agent) {
108.         if let arg = argument, !arg.isEmpty {
109.             do {
110.                 try agent.switchModel(arg)
111.                 fputs(handleModelSwitchSuccess(arg), stderr)
112.             } catch {
113.                 fputs(handleModelSwitchError(error), stderr)
114.             }
115.         } else {
116.             fputs(handleModelDisplay(model: agent.model), stderr)
117.         }
118.     }
119. 
120.     /// /cost — 显示累计 token 用量、上下文占用和预估成本。
121.     static func handleCost(usage: TokenUsage, model: String, contextTokens: Int = 0, contextWindow: Int = 0) -> String {
122.         let cost = estimateCost(usage: usage, model: model)
123.         let cacheCreation = usage.cacheCreationInputTokens ?? 0
124.         let cacheRead = usage.cacheReadInputTokens ?? 0
125.         let contextLine = ContextManager.formatContextUsage(
126.             usedTokens: contextTokens,
127.             contextWindow: contextWindow
128.         )
129.         return """
130.             Token 用量:
131.               Input:          \(usage.inputTokens)
132.               Output:         \(usage.outputTokens)
133.               Cache Creation: \(cacheCreation)
134.               Cache Read:     \(cacheRead)
135.               Total:          \(usage.totalTokens)
136.               \(contextLine)
137.             预估成本: \(cost)
138. 
139.             """
140.     }
141. 
142.     /// /config — 显示当前生效的关键配置项。
143.     static func handleConfig(
144.         model: String,
145.         maxTokens: Int,
146.         maxSteps: Int,
147.         noMemory: Bool,
148.         noSkills: Bool,
149.         permissionMode: String
150.     ) -> String {
151.         """
152.         当前配置:
153.           模型:         \(model)
154.           最大输出:     \(maxTokens) tokens
155.           最大步骤:     \(maxSteps)
156.           Memory:       \(noMemory ? "关闭" : "开启")
157.           技能系统:     \(noSkills ? "关闭" : "开启")
158.           权限模式:     \(permissionMode)
159. 
160.         """
161.     }
162. 
163.     /// /compact — 显示当前上下文状态。SDK 在 stream() 内部自动处理压缩，
164.     /// 通过 `compactBoundary` 事件通知压缩结果。
165.     static func handleCompact(contextTokens: Int = 0, contextWindow: Int = 0) -> String {
166.         ContextManager.formatCompactStatus(
167.             usedTokens: contextTokens,
168.             contextWindow: contextWindow
169.         )
170.     }
171. 
172.     /// /resume — 处理会话恢复请求。
173.     ///
174.     /// 无参数时返回 `.none`（由 ChatCommand 显示会话列表），
175.     /// 有参数时返回 `.resumeSession(id)`（由 ChatCommand 执行 agent 重建）。
176.     static func handleResume(argument: String?) -> SlashCommandAction {
177.         guard let arg = argument, !arg.isEmpty else {
178.             // 无参数 — 通知 ChatCommand 显示会话列表
179.             return .none
180.         }
181.         return .resumeSession(arg)
182.     }
183. 
184.     /// /unknown — 未知命令提示。
185.     static func handleUnknown(_ input: String) -> String {
186.         "[axion] 未知命令: \(input)，输入 /help 查看可用命令\n"
187.     }
188. 
189.     // MARK: - Private
190. 
191.     private static func estimateCost(usage: TokenUsage, model: String) -> String {
192.         let inputCostPer1M: Double
193.         let outputCostPer1M: Double
194.         let cacheReadCostPer1M: Double
195.         if model.contains("opus") {
196.             inputCostPer1M = opusInputCostPerMTokens
197.             outputCostPer1M = opusOutputCostPerMTokens
198.             cacheReadCostPer1M = opusCacheReadCostPerMTokens
199.         } else {
200.             inputCostPer1M = sonnetInputCostPerMTokens
201.             outputCostPer1M = sonnetOutputCostPerMTokens
202.             cacheReadCostPer1M = sonnetCacheReadCostPerMTokens
203.         }
204.         let cacheRead = Double(usage.cacheReadInputTokens ?? 0)
205.         let cost = Double(usage.inputTokens) / 1_000_000 * inputCostPer1M
206.             + Double(usage.outputTokens) / 1_000_000 * outputCostPer1M
207.             + cacheRead / 1_000_000 * cacheReadCostPer1M
208.         return String(format: "$%.4f", cost)
209.     }
210. }
211.
```

### ✅ `view`

**view the file at /Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/MultiLineInputReader.swift.**

/Users/nick/CascadeProjects/axion/Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/MultiLineInputReader.swift (lines 1-260)

<details>
<summary>173 lines</summary>

```
1. import Foundation
2. 
3. /// 多行输入读取器 — 支持反斜杠续行和 bracket paste 多行粘贴。
4. ///
5. /// 在 TTY 模式下：
6. /// - **反斜杠续行**：行末 `\` + 回车 → 累积续行，显示 `...>` 提示符
7. /// - **Bracket Paste**：检测 `\x1b[200~...\x1b[201~` 包裹的粘贴内容，合并为单条输入
8. /// - **续行取消**：续行模式下空行输入 → 返回空字符串 `""`
9. ///
10. /// 非 TTY 模式（管道/重定向）下直接调用 `readLine()`，不处理上述功能。
11. ///
12. /// 所有外部依赖（`isatty`、`readLine`、`fputs`）通过构造器注入，便于测试。
13. struct MultiLineInputReader {
14. 
15.     /// Bracket paste 开始标记
16.     private static let pasteStart = "\u{1B}[200~"
17.     /// Bracket paste 结束标记
18.     private static let pasteEnd = "\u{1B}[201~"
19. 
20.     /// 是否连接到 TTY
21.     let isTTY: Bool
22. 
23.     /// 读取单行输入的闭包（注入，默认为 `readLine(strippingNewline:)`）
24.     let readLineFn: () -> String?
25. 
26.     /// 输出到 stdout 的闭包（注入，默认为 `fputs(, stdout)`）
27.     let writeStdout: (String) -> Void
28. 
29.     /// 输出到 stderr 的闭包（注入，默认为 `fputs(, stderr)`）
30.     let writeStderr: (String) -> Void
31. 
32.     // MARK: - Init
33. 
34.     init(
35.         isTTY: Bool = isatty(STDIN_FILENO) != 0,
36.         readLineFn: @escaping () -> String? = { readLine(strippingNewline: true) },
37.         writeStdout: @escaping (String) -> Void = { fputs($0, stdout); fflush(stdout) },
38.         writeStderr: @escaping (String) -> Void = { fputs($0, stderr); fflush(stderr) }
39.     ) {
40.         self.isTTY = isTTY
41.         self.readLineFn = readLineFn
42.         self.writeStdout = writeStdout
43.         self.writeStderr = writeStderr
44.     }
45. 
46.     // MARK: - Public API
47. 
48.     /// 读取用户输入，支持多行续行和 bracket paste。
49.     ///
50.     /// - Parameters:
51.     ///   - prompt: 主提示符（如 `axion> `）
52.     ///   - continuationPrompt: 续行提示符（如 `...> `）
53.     /// - Returns:
54.     ///   - `String?` 非 nil = 用户输入内容
55.     ///   - `nil` = EOF（stdin 关闭）
56.     ///   - `""` (空字符串) = 续行取消（用户在续行模式按了空行）
57.     func readInput(prompt: String, continuationPrompt: String) -> String? {
58.         // 非 TTY 模式：直接返回 readLine 结果，不输出提示符
59.         guard isTTY else {
60.             return readLineFn()
61.         }
62. 
63.         // TTY 模式：显示主提示符
64.         writeStdout(prompt)
65.         let firstLine = readLineFn()
66. 
67.         // EOF
68.         guard let line = firstLine else {
69.             return nil
70.         }
71. 
72.         // 检测 bracket paste
73.         if line.hasPrefix(Self.pasteStart) {
74.             return readBracketPaste(firstLine: line)
75.         }
76. 
77.         // 检测反斜杠续行
78.         if line.hasSuffix("\\") {
79.             return readContinuation(
80.                 accumulated: String(line.dropLast()),  // 去除末尾反斜杠
81.                 continuationPrompt: continuationPrompt
82.             )
83.         }
84. 
85.         // 普通输入
86.         return line
87.     }
88. 
89.     /// 启用终端 bracket paste mode（向 stderr 输出 `\x1b[?2004h`）。
90.     /// 非 TTY 模式下不输出。
91.     func enableBracketPaste() {
92.         guard isTTY else { return }
93.         writeStderr("\u{1B}[?2004h")
94.     }
95. 
96.     /// 禁用终端 bracket paste mode（向 stderr 输出 `\x1b[?2004l`）。
97.     /// 非 TTY 模式下不输出。
98.     func disableBracketPaste() {
99.         guard isTTY else { return }
100.         writeStderr("\u{1B}[?2004l")
101.     }
102. 
103.     // MARK: - Bracket Paste
104. 
105.     /// 读取 bracket paste 内容。
106.     ///
107.     /// 粘贴的多行内容被 `readLine()` 在 `\n` 处拆分成多次调用。
108.     /// 策略：累积每一行，直到遇到以 `\x1b[201~` 结尾的行。
109.     private func readBracketPaste(firstLine: String) -> String {
110.         // 去除开头的 paste start 标记
111.         let firstContent = String(firstLine.dropFirst(Self.pasteStart.count))
112. 
113.         // 检查是否单行就包含了 paste end
114.         if firstContent.hasSuffix(Self.pasteEnd) {
115.             let content = String(firstContent.dropLast(Self.pasteEnd.count))
116.             return content
117.         }
118. 
119.         // 多行累积
120.         var lines = [firstContent]
121.         while let nextLine = readLineFn() {
122.             if nextLine.hasSuffix(Self.pasteEnd) {
123.                 let lastContent = String(nextLine.dropLast(Self.pasteEnd.count))
124.                 if !lastContent.isEmpty {
125.                     lines.append(lastContent)
126.                 }
127.                 break
128.             }
129.             lines.append(nextLine)
130.         }
131.         return lines.joined(separator: "\n")
132.     }
133. 
134.     // MARK: - Continuation
135. 
136.     /// 读取续行输入。
137.     ///
138.     /// - Parameters:
139.     ///   - accumulated: 已累积的内容（已去除末尾反斜杠）
140.     ///   - continuationPrompt: 续行提示符
141.     /// - Returns:
142.     ///   - 合并后的完整字符串
143.     ///   - `""` 空字符串表示续行取消
144.     private func readContinuation(accumulated: String, continuationPrompt: String) -> String {
145.         var parts = [accumulated]
146. 
147.         while true {
148.             // 显示续行提示符
149.             writeStdout(continuationPrompt)
150. 
151.             guard let line = readLineFn() else {
152.                 // EOF：返回已累积内容
153.                 return parts.joined(separator: "\n")
154.             }
155. 
156.             // 续行取消：空行输入
157.             if line.isEmpty {
158.                 return ""
159.             }
160. 
161.             // 继续续行：行末有反斜杠
162.             if line.hasSuffix("\\") {
163.                 parts.append(String(line.dropLast()))
164.                 continue
165.             }
166. 
167.             // 正常结束
168.             parts.append(line)
169.             return parts.joined(separator: "\n")
170.         }
171.     }
172. }
173.
```

</details>

<summary>122 lines</summary>

```
1. import Foundation
2. import OpenAgentSDK
3. 
4. /// Handles tool permission checks for the interactive chat REPL.
5. ///
6. /// Provides a ``CanUseToolFn`` closure that:
7. /// - Auto-allows read-only tools (Read, Grep, Glob, etc.)
8. /// - Auto-allows Write/Edit in acceptEdits mode
9. /// - Auto-allows all tools in bypassPermissions mode
10. /// - Prompts the user for confirmation on other non-read-only tools
11. /// - Denies all non-read-only tools in non-TTY environments (safe default)
12. enum PermissionHandler {
13. 
14.     // MARK: - Public API
15. 
16.     /// Creates a ``CanUseToolFn`` closure for SDK tool permission checks.
17.     ///
18.     /// - Parameters:
19.     ///   - mode: The effective permission mode for this session.
20.     ///   - isTTY: Whether stdin is connected to a TTY (defaults to real `isatty` check).
21.     ///   - readUserInput: Closure to read a line of user input (injectable for testing).
22.     /// - Returns: A ``CanUseToolFn`` closure suitable for ``AgentOptions/canUseTool``.
23.     static func createCanUseTool(
24.         mode: PermissionMode,
25.         isTTY: Bool = isatty(STDIN_FILENO) != 0,
26.         readUserInput: @Sendable @escaping () -> String? = { readLine(strippingNewline: true) }
27.     ) -> CanUseToolFn {
28.         return { tool, input, _ in
29.             // AC4: Read-only tools auto-allow in all modes
30.             if tool.isReadOnly {
31.                 return .allow()
32.             }
33. 
34.             // AC3: bypassPermissions — auto-allow everything
35.             if mode == .bypassPermissions {
36.                 return .allow()
37.             }
38. 
39.             // AC2: acceptEdits — auto-allow Write/Edit, others need confirmation
40.             if mode == .acceptEdits {
41.                 if tool.name == "Write" || tool.name == "Edit" {
42.                     return .allow()
43.                 }
44.                 // Fall through to prompt for Bash etc.
45.             }
46. 
47.             // AC1: default mode — prompt user for non-read-only tools
48.             // Safety: non-TTY (pipe/redirect) → deny (cannot interact)
49.             if !isTTY {
50.                 return .deny("非终端环境，拒绝执行 \(tool.name)")
51.             }
52. 
53.             // Show prompt on stderr, read from stdin
54.             let description = extractDescription(tool: tool, input: input)
55.             fputs("⚠️  \(tool.name): \(description)\n   允许？[y/n] ", stderr)
56.             fflush(stderr)
57. 
58.             guard let response = readUserInput()?.lowercased() else {
59.                 return .deny("无法读取用户输入")
60.             }
61. 
62.             if response == "y" || response == "yes" {
63.                 return .allow()
64.             } else {
65.                 return .deny("用户拒绝执行 \(tool.name)")
66.             }
67.         }
68.     }
69. 
70.     // MARK: - Description Extraction
71. 
72.     /// Extracts a human-readable description from tool input for the permission prompt.
73.     ///
74.     /// - Bash → command parameter
75.     /// - Write → "写入 {file_path}"
76.     /// - Edit → "编辑 {file_path}"
77.     /// - Others → tool name
78.     static func extractDescription(tool: ToolProtocol, input: Any) -> String {
79.         guard let dict = input as? [String: Any] else {
80.             return tool.name
81.         }
82.         switch tool.name {
83.         case "Bash":
84.             return dict["command"] as? String ?? tool.name
85.         case "Write":
86.             return "写入 \(dict["file_path"] as? String ?? "文件")"
87.         case "Edit":
88.             return "编辑 \(dict["file_path"] as? String ?? "文件")"
89.         default:
90.             return tool.name
91.         }
92.     }
93. 
94.     // MARK: - Mode Resolution
95. 
96.     /// Computes the effective ``PermissionMode`` from CLI flags.
97.     static func resolveMode(
98.         acceptEdits: Bool,
99.         dangerouslySkipPermissions: Bool
100.     ) -> PermissionMode {
101.         if dangerouslySkipPermissions {
102.             return .bypassPermissions
103.         }
104.         if acceptEdits {
105.             return .acceptEdits
106.         }
107.         return .default
108.     }
109. 
110.     /// Returns a human-readable display name for the permission mode (used in /config).
111.     static func modeDisplayName(_ mode: PermissionMode) -> String {
112.         switch mode {
113.         case .default: return "default"
114.         case .acceptEdits: return "acceptEdits"
115.         case .bypassPermissions: return "bypassPermissions"
116.         case .plan: return "plan"
117.         case .dontAsk: return "dontAsk"
118.         case .auto: return "auto"
119.         }
120.     }
121. }
122.
```

</details>

命令、多行输入、上下文管理、会话恢复。这些能力让 Axion 从单次 `run` 进化到多轮对话，但整体仍然更像一个“增强版 REPL”，还不是一个真正**顺手、可扫读、可控、可连续工作**的终端 coding agent。\n+\n+本 Epic 的目标不是增加新的 agent 核心能力，而是把 **已有能力做成更高质量的交互层**：\n+\n+1. **更好读**：用户消息、AI 回复、工具动作、审批请求一眼区分\n+2. **更好输**：减少“必须整句输入完再提交”的摩擦，补齐历史、排队、搜索、外部编辑\n+3. **更好控**：slash 命令、审批、会话切换、旁路探索都更易发现、更低心智负担\n+4. **更连续**：长会话、忙时补充、临时分叉、恢复上下文都更自然\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 设计原则\n+\n+### 1. 保持 Axion 的终端 REPL 改造成 ratatui 全屏应用\n+- 不引入 pets / theme picker / realtime voice / apps / plugins 等与 coding agent 主路径弱相关能力\n+\n+### 2. 先建立“语义化交互层”，再补高级体验\n+\n+彩色圆点、消息块、审批样式、状态行、命令面板都应共享一套视觉语义，而不是 story 各自输出一套格式。\n+\n+### 3. 键盘优先，但必须优雅降级\n+\n+TTY 环境下可用快捷键、popup、raw-input；非 TTY / pipe 模式下保留现有简单行为，不影响脚本化使用。\n+\n+### 4. 只迁移对 Axion 真正有价值的 Codex 体验\n+\n+只吸收这些维度：\n+- command discoverability\n+- approval 输入历史搜索、外部编辑、忙时排队编辑\n+- `@file` / `/diff` / richer `/status`\n+- `/new`、`/fork`、`/archive`、`/side`\n+\n+---\n+\n+## Codex 交互体验盘点（本 Epic 的输入）\n+\n+| Codex 体验 | 价值 | Codex 参考 |\n+|---|---|---|\n+| slash / 详情查看 | 安全且不烦人 | `codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/approval_overlay.rs` |\n+| Ctrl+R 历史搜索 + Up/Down 历史回填 | prompt 输入效率高 | `codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/chat_composer/history_search.rs` |\n+| 外部编辑器回填 Scope\n+\n+- 消息角色视觉语义（包括你提到的**左侧不同颜色实心圆点**）\n+- 输入器升级（从 `readLine` 型输入迈向可处理 key event 的轻量 composer）\n+- slash 命令面板与命令补全\n+- 审批交互升级\n+- 历史、外部编辑、忙时排队\n+- 工作区快捷上下文和会话流转\n+- side conversation\n+\n+### Out of Scope\n+\n+- 语音、图片、宠物、主题商店、插件市场\n+- IDE 集成上下文\n+- 多 agent 线程切换器\n+- 全屏 TUI 重写\n+\n+---\n+\n+## Story 依赖关系\n+\n+```text\n+38.0 轻量 Composer 输入基础\n+  ├──► 38.2 Slash 命令面板与补全\n+  ├──► 38.3 审批中心 v2\n+  ├──► 38.4 Composer 效率增强\n+  ├──► 38.5 Busy-turn 输入排队\n+  ├──► 38.6 工作区快捷上下文\n+  ├──► 38.7 会话工作流\n+  └──► 38.8 Side Conversation\n+\n+38.1 对话视觉语义层 ── 独立，可尽早交付\n+```\n+\n+**建议实施顺序：** 38.1 → 38.0 → 38.2 → 38.3 → 38.4 → 38.5 → 38.6 → 38.7 → 38.8\n+\n+---\n+\n+## Stories\n+\n+### Story 38.0: 轻量 Composer 输入基础\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want chat 输入从 `readLine()` 升级为可处理 key event 的轻量 composer,  \n+So that slash popup、历史搜索、快捷键、排队编辑等能力有统一承载层。\n+\n+**为什么先做：** 当前 `MultiLineInputReader` 仍是行读取模型，适合 multiline / paste，但不适合命令 popup、历史搜索、快捷键式交互。若继续在 `readLine()` 之上叠功能，后续 story 会越来越脆弱。\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户在 TTY 中运行 `axion`  \n+**When** 输入普通文本  \n+**Then** 行为与当前 chat 基本一致  \n+**And** 仍支持多行输入和 bracket paste\n+\n+**Given** 用户按下快捷键（如 Up / Down / Ctrl+R / Ctrl+G）  \n+**When** composer 处理输入  \n+**Then** 不需要等待整行提交后再响应  \n+**And** 非 TTY 模式下自动降级到现有 `readLine()` 路径\n+\n+**实现参考：**\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/MultiLineInputReader.swift`\n+- 新增 `ChatComposer.swift` / `KeyEventReader.swift`（命名待定）\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.1: 对话视觉语义层\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 用户提问、AI 回复、工具事件、审批事件在终端里有稳定的视觉标识,  \n+So that 长对话中我能快速扫读上下文，而不是面对一整段连续文本。\n+\n+**核心设计：**\n+\n+- 在消息左侧引入**语义圆点**：\n+  - 用户：蓝色 `●`\n+  - AI：绿色 `●`\n+  - Tool：黄色 `●`\n+  - Approval / Warning：红色 `●`\n+- 同一轮 assistant 输出在视觉上组成一个 block\n+- tool/result/approval 使用统一的缩进和标题样式\n+- 非 TTY / 不支持 ANSI 时自动回退为纯文本前缀\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户发送一条消息  \n+**When** 该消息进入 transcript  \n+**Then** 终端左侧显示用户角色圆点  \n+**And** 该轮消息主体与后续 assistant/tool block 明确分层\n+\n+**Given** assistant 开始回复  \n+**When** 流式输出进行中  \n+**Then** assistant 文本以 AI 角色样式输出  \n+**And** 与工具调用、错误、审批请求有可区分视觉语义\n+\n+**Given** tool call / tool result / approval request  \n+**When** 输出到终端  \n+**Then** 左侧或标题区域有固定语义标识  \n+**And** 颜色和图标的含义在整场会话中保持一致\n+\n+**实现参考：**\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/ChatOutputFormatter.swift`\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/MarkdownTerminalRenderer.swift`\n+- 新增 `ChatTheme.swift` / `TranscriptRenderer.swift`（命名待定）\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.2: Slash 命令面板与补全\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 输入 `/` 时看到命令列表、描述和筛选结果,  \n+So that 我不必记住所有 slash 命令。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- 命令枚举与描述：`codex-rs/tui/src/slash_command.rs`\n+- popup 过滤：`codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/command_popup.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户在空输入或行首输入 `/`  \n+**When** composer 进入 slash 模式  \n+**Then** 显示可用命令列表和简要描述\n+\n+**Given** 用户继续输入 `/re`  \n+**When** 命令面板过滤  \n+**Then** 只显示匹配命令（如 `/resume`、未来的 `/review`）  \n+**And** Enter 可补全当前高亮项\n+\n+**Given** 命令支持 inline 参数（如 `/resume <id>`）  \n+**When** 用户完成命令名  \n+**Then** 参数区仍可继续编辑  \n+**And** 不把整条命令误判为普通消息\n+\n+**实现参考：**\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/SlashCommand.swift`\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/SlashCommandHandler.swift`\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.3: 审批中心 v2\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 在危险操作确认时拥有一次允许、会话允许、命令前缀允许和查看详情等选择,  \n+So that 安全性和操作流畅度能同时兼顾。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- `codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/approval_overlay.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** agent 要执行危险 Bash 命令  \n+**When** 审批触发  \n+**Then** 用户至少可以选择：\n+1. 仅本次允许\n+2. 本会话对相同命令允许\n+3. 对命令前缀允许（如 `git status` / `swift test --filter ...`）\n+4. 拒绝\n+\n+**Given** agent 要修改文件  \n+**When** 审批触发  \n+**Then** 用户可以查看目标文件、修改摘要或 diff 摘要  \n+**And** 不需要在“盲批”状态下做决定\n+\n+**Given** 非 TTY 环境  \n+**When** 审批触发  \n+**Then** 保持当前安全默认：拒绝危险操作\n+\n+**实现参考：**\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Chat/PermissionHandler.swift`\n+- `Sources/AxionCLI/Commands/ChatCommand.swift`\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.4: Composer 效率增强\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 用历史浏览、Ctrl+R 搜索和外部编辑器快速修改 prompt,  \n+So that 长 prompt 和重复 prompt 的输入成本大幅下降。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- 历史搜索：`codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/chat_composer/history_search.rs`\n+- 外部编辑器：`codex-rs/tui/src/external_editor.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户按 Up / Down  \n+**When** composer 中没有正在编辑的复杂多行草稿  \n+**Then** 可以回填和浏览最近历史消息\n+\n+**Given** 用户按 Ctrl+R  \n+**When** 输入搜索关键字  \n+**Then** 可以按时间倒序搜索历史 prompt  \n+**And** Enter 采纳当前匹配项作为可编辑草稿  \n+**And** Esc / Ctrl+C 可取消搜索并恢复原草稿\n+\n+**Given** 用户按 Ctrl+G  \n+**When** 本机设置了 `VISUAL` 或 `EDITOR`  \n+**Then** Axion 在外部编辑器打开当前草稿  \n+**And** 保存退出后内容回填到 composer\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.5: Busy-turn 输入排队\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 在 agent 还在执行时先输入下一条消息并排队,  \n+So that 我不用傻等当前回合结束才能补充信息。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- `codex-rs/tui/src/chatwidget/input_queue.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 当前 turn 正在执行  \n+**When** 用户提交新的普通消息  \n+**Then** 该消息进入 queued 状态  \n+**And** 终端明确显示“已排队”的反馈\n+\n+**Given** 当前 turn 结束  \n+**When** 队列里有待发送消息  \n+**Then** 下一条消息自动进入执行  \n+**And** 队列顺序保持 FIFO\n+\n+**Given** 用户发现排队消息写错了  \n+**When** 触发“编辑最近排队消息”快捷键  \n+**Then** 最近一条排队消息恢复到 composer 中可编辑\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.6: 工作区快捷上下文\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 用最短路径把 repo 里的关键上下文送进会话,  \n+So that 我不必手写冗长 prompt 描述文件和 diff。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- `@` 文件搜索：`codex-rs/tui/src/bottom_pane/file_search_popup.rs`\n+- richer status：`codex-rs/tui/src/status/card.rs`\n+- `/diff` 命令参考：`codex-rs/tui/src/slash_command.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `@`  \n+**When** 开始输入文件名  \n+**Then** 弹出文件候选列表  \n+**And** 选中后把路径插入当前消息\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `/diff`  \n+**When** 命令执行  \n+**Then** 终端展示当前 git diff 摘要  \n+**And** 用户可将其作为当前会话的快捷上下文\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `/status`  \n+**When** 命令执行  \n+**Then** 显示当前模型、权限模式、session、context 使用量、cwd 等核心状态  \n+**And** 比现有 `/config` 更贴近“当前会话状态卡”\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.7: 会话工作流\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 有 `/new`、`/fork`、`/archive` 这类会话命令,  \n+So that 我可以自然地开始新话题、分叉旧思路或整理会话。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- `new / fork / archive / resume`：`codex-rs/tui/src/slash_command.rs`\n+- session picker / fork：`codex-rs/tui/src/resume_picker.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `/new`  \n+**When** 命令执行  \n+**Then** 开始一个新会话  \n+**And** 当前会话保留可恢复\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `/fork`  \n+**When** 命令执行  \n+**Then** 从当前会话分叉出一个新 session  \n+**And** 继承当前上下文但后续消息互不污染\n+\n+**Given** 用户输入 `/archive`  \n+**When** 命令执行  \n+**Then** 当前会话被归档  \n+**And** 默认 resume 列表中不优先显示归档会话\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Story 38.8: Side Conversation\n+\n+As a Axion CLI 用户,  \n+I want 在主线程之外临时开一个 side conversation 提问或探索,  \n+So that 我可以查一个问题、试一个思路，而不污染主任务线程。\n+\n+**Codex 对标：**\n+- `codex-rs/tui/src/app/side.rs`\n+\n+**Acceptance Criteria：**\n+\n+**Given** 当前主会话已经开始  \n+**When** 用户输入 `/side <question>`  \n+**Then** Axion 创建一个临时 side session  \n+**And** 明确告诉 agent：主线程历史只作参考，不是当前 side 任务\n+\n+**Given** 用户在 side 会话中进行轻量探索  \n+**When** side 会话结束  \n+**Then** 用户能清晰返回主线程  \n+**And** side 会话默认不改动主线程的目标和执行节奏\n+\n+**Given** 用户未明确要求修改  \n+**When** side conversation 中执行动作  \n+**Then** 默认仅允许非破坏性探索，不主动修改工作区\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 非目标与延后项\n+\n+以下 Codex 能力本 Epic 明确不搬：\n+\n+- `pets` / `theme` / `realtime`\n+- apps / plugins / rollout / feedback\n+- 多 agent 线程切换器\n+- 图片附件\n+- 全屏 transcript overlay\n+\n+这些能力可以在未来单独评估，但不应干扰 Epic 38 的核心目标：**把 Axion chat 做成一个顺手的 terminal coding conversation surface。**\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 产品结论\n+\n+Epic 37 定义的是 **“Axion 有了交互 chat mode”**。  \n+Epic 38 定义的是 **“Axion 的交互 chat mode 值得长期使用”**。\n+\n+如果说 Epic 37 把 Axion 从 `run` 带到了 `chat`，那么 Epic 38 要把 Axion 从 **“能对话”** 带到 **“好对话”**。\n*** End Patch\n"
````

</details>
